# AGENTS.md instructions for D:\demo1\papaweb

<INSTRUCTIONS>
# AGENTS.md

## 1) 目标
本文件定义 papaweb 团队开发协作规则，适用于本地团队与所有自动化代理。

## 2) 分支模型
- main：生产/发布分支，只接收经过验证的发布变更。
- dev：日常集成分支，所有功能先合入此分支。
- feature/*：新功能分支，从 dev 切出，合回 dev。
- fix/*：缺陷修复分支，从 dev 切出，合回 dev。
- release/*：发布准备分支，从 dev 切出；验证通过后 PR 合入 main，随后回合 dev。
- hotfix/*：线上紧急修复分支，从 main 切出，先合入 main，再回合 dev。

## 3) 推送与 PR 规则（强约束）
- 禁止直接 push 到 main。
- 禁止直接 push 到 dev。
- 所有日常开发变更必须通过 PR 合入 dev。
- main 只允许来自 release/ 或 hotfix/ 的 PR。
- 每个 PR 至少 1 名 reviewer 审核通过后才能合并。

## 4) CI / E2E 准入规则
- PR 合并到 dev 前，必须满足：
- ci 检查通过（单元测试、静态检查）。
- e2e 检查通过（端到端关键路径）。
- 任一检查失败，禁止合并。
- 禁止以“先合并后补测”为理由绕过。

## 5) TDD（测试驱动开发）规则
- 必须执行 Red -> Green -> Refactor 三步：
- Red：先写测试并确认失败。
- Green：写最小实现让测试通过。
- Refactor：重构代码并保持测试持续通过。
- 修复 bug 时，必须先补回归测试，再改业务代码。
- 新增功能 PR，至少包含：
- 1 个单元测试。
- 1 个集成测试或 E2E 用例（覆盖主流程）。
- 禁止删除/跳过测试来“凑绿灯”。

## 6) PR 必填信息
- 变更目的与范围。
- 验收标准（可观察结果）。
- 测试证据（执行命令与结果）。
- 风险点与回滚方案。
- 若影响使用方式，需同步更新文档。

## 7) 合并策略
- 默认使用 Squash merge，保持历史清晰。
- Commit message 建议使用 Conventional Commits（如 feat:, fix:, chore:）。

## 8) 本地防护建议（必配）
- 所有人本地安装 pre-push hook，拦截推送到 main/dev。
- 推荐规则：若目标分支是 main 或 dev，直接拒绝并提示走 PR。

## 9) 紧急例外流程
- 仅 hotfix/* 可走紧急流程。
- 需在 PR 描述中写明原因、风险、回滚步骤。
- 紧急修复合入 main 后，必须在 24 小时内回合到 dev 并补齐测试。

## Skills
A skill is a set of local instructions to follow that is stored in a SKILL.md file. Below is the list of skills that can be used. Each entry includes a name, description, and file path so you can open the source for full instructions when using a specific skill.
### Available skills
- skill-creator: Guide for creating effective skills. This skill should be used when users want to create a new skill (or update an existing skill) that extends Codex's capabilities with specialized knowledge, workflows, or tool integrations. (file: C:/Users/ai/.codex/skills/.system/skill-creator/SKILL.md)
- skill-installer: Install Codex skills into $CODEX_HOME/skills from a curated list or a GitHub repo path. Use when a user asks to list installable skills, install a curated skill, or install a skill from another repo (including private repos). (file: C:/Users/ai/.codex/skills/.system/skill-installer/SKILL.md)
### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with $SkillName or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
1) After deciding to use a skill, open its SKILL.md. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
2) When SKILL.md references relative paths (e.g., scripts/foo.py), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
3) If SKILL.md points to extra folders such as references/, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
4) If scripts/ exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
5) If assets/ or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
- If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
- Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
- Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
- Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from SKILL.md unless you're blocked.
- When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.
</INSTRUCTIONS>

<collaboration_mode># Collaboration Mode: Default

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different <collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode> change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The request_user_input tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.
</collaboration_mode>

  "user_instructions": "# AGENTS.md\n\n## 1) 目标\n本文件定义 `papaweb` 团队开发协作规则，适用于本地团队与所有自动化代理。\n\n## 2) 分支模型\n- `main`：生产/发布分支，只接收经过验证的发布变更。\n- `dev`：日常集成分支，所有功能先合入此分支。\n- `feature/*`：新功能分支，从 `dev` 切出，合回 `dev`。\n- `fix/*`：缺陷修复分支，从 `dev` 切出，合回 `dev`。\n- `release/*`：发布准备分支，从 `dev` 切出；验证通过后 PR 合入 `main`，随后回合 `dev`。\n- `hotfix/*`：线上紧急修复分支，从 `main` 切出，先合入 `main`，再回合 `dev`。\n\n## 3) 推送与 PR 规则（强约束）\n- 禁止直接 push 到 `main`。\n- 禁止直接 push 到 `dev`。\n- 所有日常开发变更必须通过 PR 合入 `dev`。\n- `main` 只允许来自 `release/*` 或 `hotfix/*` 的 PR。\n- 每个 PR 至少 1 名 reviewer 审核通过后才能合并。\n\n## 4) CI / E2E 准入规则\n- PR 合并到 `dev` 前，必须满足：\n- `ci` 检查通过（单元测试、静态检查）。\n- `e2e` 检查通过（端到端关键路径）。\n- 任一检查失败，禁止合并。\n- 禁止以“先合并后补测”为理由绕过。\n\n## 5) TDD（测试驱动开发）规则\n- 必须执行 `Red -> Green -> Refactor` 三步：\n- `Red`：先写测试并确认失败。\n- `Green`：写最小实现让测试通过。\n- `Refactor`：重构代码并保持测试持续通过。\n- 修复 bug 时，必须先补回归测试，再改业务代码。\n- 新增功能 PR，至少包含：\n- 1 个单元测试。\n- 1 个集成测试或 E2E 用例（覆盖主流程）。\n- 禁止删除/跳过测试来“凑绿灯”。\n\n## 6) PR 必填信息\n- 变更目的与范围。\n- 验收标准（可观察结果）。\n- 测试证据（执行命令与结果）。\n- 风险点与回滚方案。\n- 若影响使用方式，需同步更新文档。\n\n## 7) 合并策略\n- 默认使用 `Squash merge`，保持历史清晰。\n- Commit message 建议使用 Conventional Commits（如 `feat:`, `fix:`, `chore:`）。\n\n## 8) 本地防护建议（必配）\n- 所有人本地安装 `pre-push` hook，拦截推送到 `main`/`dev`。\n- 推荐规则：若目标分支是 `main` 或 `dev`，直接拒绝并提示走 PR。\n\n## 9) 紧急例外流程\n- 仅 `hotfix/*` 可走紧急流程。\n- 需在 PR 描述中写明原因、风险、回滚步骤。\n- 紧急修复合入 `main` 后，必须在 24 小时内回合到 `dev` 并补齐测试。\n\n\n## Skills\nA skill is a set of local instructions to follow that is stored in a `SKILL.md` file. import process from "node:process";
import express from "express";
import {
  createPgPool,
  createRedisClient,
  enqueueSeedBatch,
  ensurePlatformSchema,
  getPlatformConfig,
  loadSeedPlan,
  log,
} from "@papaweb/shared";

const serviceName = "query-api";
const config = getPlatformConfig();
const pg = createPgPool(config.db);
const redis = createRedisClient(config.redis);
const app = express();
app.use(express.json({ limit: "256kb" }));

app.get("/healthz", async (_req, res) => {
  try {
    await pg.query("SELECT 1");
    res.status(200).json({ status: "ok", service: serviceName });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({
      status: "error",
      message: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
    });
  }
});

app.get("/api/v1/tools", async (req, res) => {
  const limit = normalizeLimit(req.query.limit, 20, 200);
  const rows = await pg.query(
    `SELECT id, canonical_url, title, summary, source_id, quality_score, trace_id, published_at, updated_at
     FROM gold_tool_entities
     ORDER BY published_at DESC
     LIMIT $1`,
    [limit]
  );
  res.json({ items: rows.rows, count: rows.rowCount });
});

app.get("/api/v1/tasks", async (req, res) => {
  const limit = normalizeLimit(req.query.limit, 20, 200);
  const rows = await pg.query(
    `SELECT id, job_id, trace_id, source_id, url, stage, status, http_status, error, published, created_at, updated_at
     FROM crawl_tasks
     ORDER BY created_at DESC
     LIMIT $1`,
    [limit]
  );
  res.json({ items: rows.rows, count: rows.rowCount });
});

app.get("/api/v1/metrics", async (_req, res) => {
  const row = (
    await pg.query(
      `SELECT
         COUNT(*) AS total_tasks,
         COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'published') AS published_tasks,
         COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'quality_rejected') AS quality_rejected_tasks,
         COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'fetch_failed') AS fetch_failed_tasks,
         COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'queued_fetch') AS queued_fetch_tasks,
         COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'queued_quality') AS queued_quality_tasks,
         COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'queued_publish') AS queued_publish_tasks
       FROM crawl_tasks`
    )
  ).rows[0];

  const published = Number(row.published_tasks ?? 0);
  const rejected = Number(row.quality_rejected_tasks ?? 0);
  const attempts = published + rejected;
  const publishPassRate = attempts > 0 ? Number((published / attempts).toFixed(4)) : 0;

  res.json({
    totalTasks: Number(row.total_tasks ?? 0),
    publishedTasks: published,
    qualityRejectedTasks: rejected,
    fetchFailedTasks: Number(row.fetch_failed_tasks ?? 0),
    queuedFetchTasks: Number(row.queued_fetch_tasks ?? 0),
    queuedQualityTasks: Number(row.queued_quality_tasks ?? 0),
    queuedPublishTasks: Number(row.queued_publish_tasks ?? 0),
    publishPassRate,
  });
});

app.get("/api/v1/source-sites", async (_req, res) => {
  const rows = await pg.query(
    `SELECT id, name, base_url, enabled, meta, updated_at
     FROM source_sites
     ORDER BY id ASC`
  );
  res.json({ items: rows.rows, count: rows.rowCount });
});

app.post("/api/v1/pipeline/seed-run", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const body = req.body && typeof req.body === "object" ? req.body : {};
    const seedUrls = normalizeArray(body.seedUrls);
    const sourceIds = normalizeArray(body.sourceIds);
    const requestedBy = normalizeString(body.requestedBy) || "query-api";
    const reason = normalizeString(body.reason) || "manual_trigger";
    const sourceId = normalizeString(body.sourceId) || config.sourceId;

    const seedPlan = await loadSeedPlan({
      seedUrls: seedUrls.length > 0 ? seedUrls : config.seedUrls,
      sourceId,
      sourceIds: sourceIds.length > 0 ? sourceIds : config.sourceIds,
      sourceSitesConfigPath: config.sourceSitesConfigPath,
    });

    const result = await enqueueSeedBatch(pg, redis, seedPlan, {
      queues: config.queues,
      workerName: serviceName,
      requestedBy,
      reason,
    });

    res.status(202).json({
      accepted: true,
      ...result,
      requestedBy,
      reason,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({
      accepted: false,
      message: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
    });
  }
});

async function main() {
  await ensurePlatformSchema(pg);
  const server = app.listen(config.queryApiPort, () => {
    log(serviceName, "info", "query-api started", { port: config.queryApiPort });
  });

  const shutdown = async () => {
    server.close(async () => {
      await redis.quit();
      await pg.end();
      process.exit(0);
    });
  };
  process.on("SIGINT", shutdown);
  process.on("SIGTERM", shutdown);
}

main().catch((error) => {
  log(serviceName, "error", "query-api crashed", {
    error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
  });
  process.exit(1);
});

function normalizeLimit(value, defaultValue, max) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n) || n <= 0) return defaultValue;
  return Math.min(Math.floor(n), max);
}

function normalizeArray(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.map((item) => String(item).trim()).filter(Boolean);
  }
  if (typeof value === "string") {
    return value
      .split(",")
      .map((item) => item.trim())
      .filter(Boolean);
  }
  return [];
}

function normalizeString(value) {
  if (typeof value !== "string") return "";
  return value.trim();
}

const serviceName = "worker-fetch-http";
const config = getPlatformConfig();
let stopping = false;

process.on("SIGINT", () => {
  stopping = true;
});
process.on("SIGTERM", () => {
  stopping = true;
});

async function fetchHtml(url) {
  const ctrl = new AbortController();
  const timer = setTimeout(() => ctrl.abort(), config.fetchTimeoutMs);
  try {
    const res = await fetch(url, {
      method: "GET",
      redirect: "follow",
      signal: ctrl.signal,
      headers: {
        "user-agent": "papaweb-platform/0.1",
      },
    });
    const text = await res.text();
    return {
      ok: res.ok,
      status: res.status,
      html: text.slice(0, 250000),
      error: null,
    };
  } catch (error) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      status: 0,
      html: "",
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
    };
  } finally {
    clearTimeout(timer);
  }
}

async function processMessage(pg, redis, message) {
  const traceId = requireString(message.traceId, "traceId");
  const jobId = requireString(message.jobId, "jobId");
  const taskId = requireString(message.taskId, "taskId");
  const sourceId = requireString(message.sourceId, "sourceId");
  const url = requireString(message.url, "url");

  await pg.query(
    `UPDATE crawl_tasks
     SET stage = $2, status = $3, updated_at = NOW()
     WHERE id = $1`,
    [taskId, TASK_STAGES.fetch, TASK_STATUS.fetching]
  );

  const fetched = await fetchHtml(url);
  if (!fetched.ok) {
    await pg.query(
      `UPDATE crawl_tasks
       SET stage = $2, status = $3, error = $4, http_status = $5, updated_at = NOW()
       WHERE id = $1`,
      [taskId, TASK_STAGES.fetch, TASK_STATUS.fetchFailed, fetched.error, fetched.status]
    );
    await pg.query(
      `INSERT INTO url_state(url, status, last_http_status, last_error, last_fetched_at, updated_at)
       VALUES($1, $2, $3, $4, NOW(), NOW())
       ON CONFLICT(url)
       DO UPDATE SET
         status = EXCLUDED.status,
         last_http_status = EXCLUDED.last_http_status,
         last_error = EXCLUDED.last_error,
         last_fetched_at = NOW(),
         updated_at = NOW()`,
      [url, "fetch_failed", fetched.status, fetched.error]
    );
    await recordPipelineEvent(pg, {
      traceId,
      jobId,
      taskId,
      worker: serviceName,
      name: "fetch_failed",
      payload: { url, httpStatus: fetched.status, error: fetched.error },
    });
    return;
  }

  await pg.query(
    `UPDATE crawl_tasks
     SET stage = $2, status = $3, http_status = $4, raw_html = $5, error = NULL, updated_at = NOW()
     WHERE id = $1`,
    [taskId, TASK_STAGES.fetch, TASK_STATUS.queuedNormalize, fetched.status, fetched.html]
  );
  await pg.query(
    `INSERT INTO url_state(url, status, last_http_status, last_error, last_fetched_at, updated_at)
     VALUES($1, $2, $3, NULL, NOW(), NOW())
     ON CONFLICT(url)
     DO UPDATE SET
       status = EXCLUDED.status,
       last_http_status = EXCLUDED.last_http_status,
       last_error = NULL,
       last_fetched_at = NOW(),
       updated_at = NOW()`,
    [url, "fetched", fetched.status]
  );

  const next = {
    traceId,
    jobId,
    taskId,
    sourceId,
    url,
    httpStatus: fetched.status,
  };
  await pushQueue(redis, config.queues.normalize, next);
  await recordPipelineEvent(pg, {
    traceId,
    jobId,
    taskId,
    worker: serviceName,
    name: "fetch_ok",
    payload: { url, httpStatus: fetched.status, queue: config.queues.normalize },
  });
}

async function main() {
  const pg = createPgPool(config.db);
  const redis = createRedisClient(config.redis);
  try {
    await ensurePlatformSchema(pg);
    while (!stopping) {
      const message = await popQueue(redis, config.queues.fetch, config.pollSeconds);
      if (!message) {
        await sleep(150);
        continue;
      }
      try {
        await processMessage(pg, redis, message);
      } catch (error) {
        log(serviceName, "error", "process fetch message failed", {
          error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
          message,
        });
      }
    }
  } finally {
    await redis.quit();
    await pg.end();
  }
}

main().catch((error) => {
  log(serviceName, "error", "worker-fetch-http crashed", {
    error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
  });
  process.exit(1);
});

function pickTitle(html, url) {
  const titleMatch = html.match(/<title[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/title>/i);
  const title = (titleMatch?.[1] ?? "").replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim();
  if (title.length > 0) return title.slice(0, 200);
  return url;
}

function pickSummary(html) {
  const metaMatch =
    html.match(/<meta[^>]*name=["']description["'][^>]*content=["']([\s\S]*?)["'][^>]*>/i) ||
    html.match(/<meta[^>]*content=["']([\s\S]*?)["'][^>]*name=["']description["'][^>]*>/i);
  if (metaMatch?.[1]) {
    return metaMatch[1].replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim().slice(0, 300);
  }
  const bodyText = html
    .replace(/<script[\s\S]*?<\/script>/gi, " ")
    .replace(/<style[\s\S]*?<\/style>/gi, " ")
    .replace(/<[^>]+>/g, " ")
    .replace(/\s+/g, " ")
    .trim();
  return bodyText.slice(0, 300);
}

async function processMessage(pg, redis, message) {
  const traceId = requireString(message.traceId, "traceId");
  const jobId = requireString(message.jobId, "jobId");
  const taskId = requireString(message.taskId, "taskId");
  const sourceId = requireString(message.sourceId, "sourceId");
  const url = requireString(message.url, "url");
  const httpStatus = Number(message.httpStatus ?? 0);

  const taskRes = await pg.query("SELECT raw_html FROM crawl_tasks WHERE id = $1 LIMIT 1", [taskId]);
  if (taskRes.rowCount === 0) {
    throw new Error(`task not found: ${taskId}`);
  }
  const html = String(taskRes.rows[0].raw_html ?? "");
  const normalized = {
    canonicalUrl: url,
    title: pickTitle(html, url),
    summary: pickSummary(html),
    sourceId,
    normalizedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  };

  await pg.query(
    `UPDATE crawl_tasks
     SET stage = $2, status = $3, normalized = $4::jsonb, updated_at = NOW()
     WHERE id = $1`,
    [taskId, TASK_STAGES.normalize, TASK_STATUS.queuedQuality, JSON.stringify(normalized)]
  );

  await pg.query(
    `INSERT INTO url_state(url, status, last_http_status, title, summary, last_fetched_at, updated_at)
     VALUES($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, NOW(), NOW())
     ON CONFLICT(url)
     DO UPDATE SET
       status = EXCLUDED.status,
       last_http_status = EXCLUDED.last_http_status,
       title = EXCLUDED.title,
       summary = EXCLUDED.summary,
       last_fetched_at = NOW(),
       updated_at = NOW()`,
    [url, "normalized", httpStatus || null, normalized.title, normalized.summary]
  );

  const next = {
    traceId,
    jobId,
    taskId,
    sourceId,
    url,
    httpStatus,
    normalized,
  };
  await pushQueue(redis, config.queues.quality, next);
  await recordPipelineEvent(pg, {
    traceId,
    jobId,
    taskId,
    worker: serviceName,
    name: "normalized",
    payload: { queue: config.queues.quality, title: normalized.title },
  });
}

async function main() {
  const pg = createPgPool(config.db);
  const redis = createRedisClient(config.redis);
  try {
    await ensurePlatformSchema(pg);
    while (!stopping) {
      const message = await popQueue(redis, config.queues.normalize, config.pollSeconds);
      if (!message) {
        await sleep(150);
        continue;
      }
      try {
        await processMessage(pg, redis, message);
      } catch (error) {
        log(serviceName, "error", "process normalize message failed", {
          error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
          message,
        });
      }
    }
  } finally {
    await redis.quit();
    await pg.end();
  }
}

async function processMessage(pg, redis, message) {
  const traceId = requireString(message.traceId, "traceId");
  const jobId = requireString(message.jobId, "jobId");
  const taskId = requireString(message.taskId, "taskId");
  const sourceId = requireString(message.sourceId, "sourceId");
  const url = requireString(message.url, "url");
  const httpStatus = Number(message.httpStatus ?? 0);

  const taskRes = await pg.query("SELECT normalized FROM crawl_tasks WHERE id = $1 LIMIT 1", [taskId]);
  if (taskRes.rowCount === 0) {
    throw new Error(`task not found: ${taskId}`);
  }
  const normalized = taskRes.rows[0].normalized ?? {};
  const policy = await loadActivePolicy(pg, {
    ...DEFAULT_POLICY,
    version: config.qualityPolicyVersion,
  });

  const result = evaluateQuality(
    {
      title: normalized.title,
      summary: normalized.summary,
      httpStatus,
    },
    policy
  );

  await pg.query(
    `INSERT INTO quality_scores(task_id, score, threshold, pass, reasons, policy_version, created_at)
     VALUES($1, $2, $3, $4, $5::jsonb, $6, NOW())
     ON CONFLICT(task_id)
     DO UPDATE SET
       score = EXCLUDED.score,
       threshold = EXCLUDED.threshold,
       pass = EXCLUDED.pass,
       reasons = EXCLUDED.reasons,
       policy_version = EXCLUDED.policy_version,
       created_at = NOW()`,
    [taskId, result.score, result.threshold, result.pass, JSON.stringify(result.reasons), result.policyVersion]
  );

  const taskStatus = result.pass ? TASK_STATUS.queuedPublish : TASK_STATUS.qualityRejected;
  await pg.query(
    `UPDATE crawl_tasks
     SET stage = $2, status = $3, quality = $4::jsonb, updated_at = NOW()
     WHERE id = $1`,
    [taskId, TASK_STAGES.quality, taskStatus, JSON.stringify(result)]
  );

  await recordPipelineEvent(pg, {
    traceId,
    jobId,
    taskId,
    worker: serviceName,
    name: "quality_checked",
    payload: result,
  });

  if (!result.pass) {
    return;
  }

  await pushQueue(redis, config.queues.publish, {
    traceId,
    jobId,
    taskId,
    sourceId,
    url,
  });
}

async function main() {
  const pg = createPgPool(config.db);
  const redis = createRedisClient(config.redis);
  try {
    await ensurePlatformSchema(pg);
    await ensurePolicyVersion(pg, DEFAULT_POLICY.version, DEFAULT_POLICY);

    while (!stopping) {
      const message = await popQueue(redis, config.queues.quality, config.pollSeconds);
      if (!message) {
        await sleep(150);
        continue;
      }
      try {
        await processMessage(pg, redis, message);
      } catch (error) {
        log(serviceName, "error", "process quality message failed", {
          error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
          message,
        });
      }
    }
  } finally {
    await redis.quit();
    await pg.end();
  }
}

  log(serviceName, "error", "worker-quality crashed", {
    error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
  });
  process.exit(1);
});

async function processMessage(pg, message) {
  const traceId = requireString(message.traceId, "traceId");
  const jobId = requireString(message.jobId, "jobId");
  const taskId = requireString(message.taskId, "taskId");
  const sourceId = requireString(message.sourceId, "sourceId");
  const url = requireString(message.url, "url");

  const taskRes = await pg.query("SELECT normalized, quality FROM crawl_tasks WHERE id = $1 LIMIT 1", [taskId]);
  if (taskRes.rowCount === 0) {
    throw new Error(`task not found: ${taskId}`);
  }
  const task = taskRes.rows[0];
  const normalized = task.normalized ?? {};
  const quality = task.quality ?? {};

  if (!quality.pass) {
    await pg.query(
      `UPDATE crawl_tasks
       SET stage = $2, status = $3, updated_at = NOW()
       WHERE id = $1`,
      [taskId, TASK_STAGES.publish, TASK_STATUS.qualityRejected]
    );
    return;
  }

  const title = String(normalized.title ?? "").trim() || url;
  const summary = String(normalized.summary ?? "").trim();
  const canonicalUrl = String(normalized.canonicalUrl ?? url).trim();
  const qualityScore = Number(quality.score ?? 0);

  await pg.query(
    `INSERT INTO gold_tool_entities(
        canonical_url, title, summary, source_id, quality_score, trace_id, published_at, updated_at
     ) VALUES($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, NOW(), NOW())
     ON CONFLICT(canonical_url)
     DO UPDATE SET
       title = EXCLUDED.title,
       summary = EXCLUDED.summary,
       source_id = EXCLUDED.source_id,
       quality_score = EXCLUDED.quality_score,
       trace_id = EXCLUDED.trace_id,
       updated_at = NOW()`,
    [canonicalUrl, title, summary, sourceId, qualityScore, traceId]
  );

  await pg.query(
    `UPDATE crawl_tasks
     SET stage = $2, status = $3, published = TRUE, updated_at = NOW()
     WHERE id = $1`,
    [taskId, TASK_STAGES.publish, TASK_STATUS.published]
  );

  await recordPipelineEvent(pg, {
    traceId,
    jobId,
    taskId,
    worker: serviceName,
    name: "published",
    payload: {
      canonicalUrl,
      title,
      qualityScore,
    },
  });

  await pg.query(
    `UPDATE crawl_jobs j
     SET status = 'completed', updated_at = NOW()
     WHERE j.id = $1
       AND NOT EXISTS (
         SELECT 1
         FROM crawl_tasks t
         WHERE t.job_id = j.id
           AND t.status IN ('queued_fetch', 'fetching', 'queued_normalize', 'queued_quality', 'queued_publish')
       )`,
    [jobId]
  );
}

import process from "node:process";

const serviceName = "worker-seed";

process.on("SIGINT", () => {
  stopping = true;
});
process.on("SIGTERM", () => {
  stopping = true;

async function enqueueOnce(pg, redis, requestedBy, reason) {
  const seedPlan = await loadSeedPlan({
    seedUrls: config.seedUrls,
    sourceId: config.sourceId,
    sourceIds: config.sourceIds,
    sourceSitesConfigPath: config.sourceSitesConfigPath,
  });

  const result = await enqueueSeedBatch(pg, redis, seedPlan, {
    queues: config.queues,
    workerName: serviceName,
    requestedBy,
    reason,
  });

  log(serviceName, "info", "seed batch enqueued", result);
}

async function main() {
  const onceMode = process.argv.includes("--once") || parseBool(process.env.PAPAWEB_SEED_ONCE, false);
  const passiveMode = config.seedPassive;
  const pg = createPgPool(config.db);
  const redis = createRedisClient(config.redis);

  try {
    await ensurePlatformSchema(pg);
    if (onceMode) {
      await enqueueOnce(pg, redis, "worker-seed", "once");
      return;
    }

    if (passiveMode) {
      log(serviceName, "info", "seed worker in passive mode; waiting Airflow/API trigger", {
        sourceIds: config.sourceIds,
      });
      while (!stopping) {
        await sleep(2000);
      }
      return;
    }

    while (!stopping) {
      try {
        await enqueueOnce(pg, redis, "worker-seed", "loop");
      } catch (error) {
        log(serviceName, "error", "seed loop failed", {
          error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
        });
      }
      if (stopping) break;
      await sleep(config.seedIntervalSeconds * 1000);
    }
  } finally {
    await redis.quit();
    await pg.end();
  }
}

main().catch((error) => {
  log(serviceName, "error", "worker-seed crashed", {
    error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
  });
  process.exit(1);
});

const DEFAULT_SOURCE_CONFIG_PATH = "/workspace/apps/crawler/config/source-sites.v1.json";
const FALLBACK_BUSINESS_SEEDS = [
  { sourceId: "futurepedia", url: "https://www.futurepedia.io/ai-tools" },
  { sourceId: "toolify", url: "https://www.toolify.ai/" },
  { sourceId: "ainav_cn", url: "https://www.ainav.cn/" },

export function getPlatformConfig(env = process.env) {
  return {
    serviceName: env.PAPAWEB_SERVICE_NAME ?? "unknown-service",
    db: {
      host: env.PAPAWEB_DB_HOST ?? "postgres",
      port: toInt(env.PAPAWEB_DB_PORT, 5432),
      user: env.PAPAWEB_DB_USER ?? "papaweb",
      password: env.PAPAWEB_DB_PASSWORD ?? "papaweb",
      database: env.PAPAWEB_DB_NAME ?? "papaweb",
    },
    redis: {
      host: env.PAPAWEB_REDIS_HOST ?? "valkey",
      port: toInt(env.PAPAWEB_REDIS_PORT, 6379),
      db: toInt(env.PAPAWEB_REDIS_DB, 0),
    },
    queues: {
      fetch: env.PAPAWEB_FETCH_QUEUE ?? PIPELINE_QUEUES.fetch,
      normalize: env.PAPAWEB_NORMALIZE_QUEUE ?? PIPELINE_QUEUES.normalize,
      quality: env.PAPAWEB_QUALITY_QUEUE ?? PIPELINE_QUEUES.quality,
      publish: env.PAPAWEB_PUBLISH_QUEUE ?? PIPELINE_QUEUES.publish,
    },
    fetchTimeoutMs: toInt(env.PAPAWEB_FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS, 15000),
    pollSeconds: toInt(env.PAPAWEB_WORKER_POLL_SECONDS, 5),
    seedIntervalSeconds: toInt(env.PAPAWEB_SEED_INTERVAL_SECONDS, 30),
    seedPassive: parseBool(env.PAPAWEB_SEED_PASSIVE, false),
    sourceId: env.PAPAWEB_SOURCE_ID ?? "plan0-seed",
    seedUrls: splitCsv(env.PAPAWEB_SEED_URLS),
    sourceIds: splitCsv(env.PAPAWEB_SOURCE_IDS ?? DEFAULT_BUSINESS_SOURCE_IDS.join(",")),
    sourceSitesConfigPath: env.PAPAWEB_SOURCE_SITES_CONFIG ?? DEFAULT_SOURCE_CONFIG_PATH,
    queryApiPort: toInt(env.PAPAWEB_QUERY_API_PORT, 18787),
    qualityPolicyVersion: env.PAPAWEB_QUALITY_POLICY_VERSION ?? "plan0-v1",
  };
}

export function createPgPool(dbConfig) {
  return new Pool({
    host: dbConfig.host,
    port: dbConfig.port,
    user: dbConfig.user,
    password: dbConfig.password,
    database: dbConfig.database,
    max: 10,
    idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
  });
}

export function createRedisClient(redisConfig) {
  return new Redis({
    host: redisConfig.host,
    port: redisConfig.port,
    db: redisConfig.db,
    lazyConnect: false,
    maxRetriesPerRequest: null,
  });
}

export async function ensurePlatformSchema(pg) {
  const lockKey = 20260313;
  const sql = `
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS crawl_jobs (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      source_id TEXT NOT NULL,
      status TEXT NOT NULL,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
    );

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS crawl_tasks (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      job_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES crawl_jobs(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      trace_id TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
      source_id TEXT NOT NULL,
      url TEXT NOT NULL,
      stage TEXT NOT NULL,
      status TEXT NOT NULL,
      error TEXT,
      http_status INT,
      raw_html TEXT,
      normalized JSONB,
      quality JSONB,
      published BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
    );

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS url_state (
      url TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      status TEXT NOT NULL,
      last_http_status INT,
      last_error TEXT,
      title TEXT,
      summary TEXT,
      last_fetched_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
    );

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS seed_state (
      seed_url TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      source_id TEXT NOT NULL,
      last_enqueued_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
      enqueued_count BIGINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
    );

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS source_sites (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      name TEXT NOT NULL,
      base_url TEXT NOT NULL,
      enabled BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,
      meta JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
    );

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS policy_versions (
      id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
      version TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
      config JSONB NOT NULL,
      active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
    );

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS quality_scores (
      task_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY REFERENCES crawl_tasks(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      score NUMERIC(6,4) NOT NULL,
      threshold NUMERIC(6,4) NOT NULL,
      pass BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
      reasons JSONB NOT NULL,
      policy_version TEXT NOT NULL,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
    );

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS gold_tool_entities (
      id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
      canonical_url TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
      title TEXT NOT NULL,
      summary TEXT,
      source_id TEXT NOT NULL,
      quality_score NUMERIC(6,4) NOT NULL,
      trace_id TEXT NOT NULL,
      published_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
    );

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS pipeline_events (
      id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
      trace_id TEXT NOT NULL,
      job_id TEXT,
      task_id TEXT,
      worker TEXT NOT NULL,
      event TEXT NOT NULL,
      payload JSONB,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
    );

    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crawl_tasks_status ON crawl_tasks(status);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crawl_tasks_stage ON crawl_tasks(stage);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crawl_tasks_created_at ON crawl_tasks(created_at DESC);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_gold_tool_entities_published_at ON gold_tool_entities(published_at DESC);
  `;
  await pg.query("SELECT pg_advisory_lock($1)", [lockKey]);
  try {
    await pg.query(sql);
  } finally {
    await pg.query("SELECT pg_advisory_unlock($1)", [lockKey]);
  }
}

export async function ensurePolicyVersion(pg, version, config) {
  await pg.query(
    `INSERT INTO policy_versions(version, config, active)
     VALUES($1, $2::jsonb, FALSE)
     ON CONFLICT (version)
     DO UPDATE SET config = EXCLUDED.config`,
    [version, JSON.stringify(config)]
  );

  const active = await pg.query("SELECT version FROM policy_versions WHERE active = TRUE LIMIT 1");
  if (active.rowCount === 0) {
    await pg.query("UPDATE policy_versions SET active = CASE WHEN version = $1 THEN TRUE ELSE FALSE END", [version]);
  }
}

export async function loadActivePolicy(pg, fallbackPolicy) {
  const res = await pg.query(
    "SELECT version, config FROM policy_versions WHERE active = TRUE ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 1"
  );
  if (res.rowCount === 0) {
    return fallbackPolicy;
  }
  const row = res.rows[0];
  return {
    ...fallbackPolicy,
    ...(row.config && typeof row.config === "object" ? row.config : {}),
    version: row.version,
  };
}

export async function pushQueue(redis, queueName, payload) {
  await redis.lpush(queueName, encodeQueueMessage(payload));
}

export async function popQueue(redis, queueName, timeoutSeconds) {
  const row = await redis.brpop(queueName, timeoutSeconds);
  if (!row || row.length < 2) return null;
  return decodeQueueMessage(row[1]);
}

export async function recordPipelineEvent(pg, event) {
  const payload = event.payload ?? {};
  await pg.query(
    `INSERT INTO pipeline_events(trace_id, job_id, task_id, worker, event, payload, created_at)
     VALUES($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6::jsonb, NOW())`,
    [
      event.traceId,
      event.jobId ?? null,
      event.taskId ?? null,
      event.worker,
      event.name,
      JSON.stringify(payload),
    ]
  );
}

export async function loadSeedPlan(options = {}) {
  const explicitSeedUrls = Array.isArray(options.seedUrls) ? options.seedUrls : [];
  const sourceId = String(options.sourceId || "plan0-manual-seed").trim();
  const sourceIds = Array.isArray(options.sourceIds) ? options.sourceIds.filter(Boolean) : [];
  const sourceConfigPath = String(options.sourceSitesConfigPath || DEFAULT_SOURCE_CONFIG_PATH).trim();

  if (explicitSeedUrls.length > 0) {
    return {
      targets: dedupeSeedTargets(
        explicitSeedUrls.map((url) => ({
          sourceId,
          url,
        }))
      ),
      sourceSites: [],
      mode: "explicit_urls",
    };
  }

  const parsed = await loadSourceSitesFromFile(sourceConfigPath, sourceIds);
  if (parsed.targets.length > 0) {
    return parsed;
  }

  return {
    targets: FALLBACK_BUSINESS_SEEDS,
    sourceSites: FALLBACK_BUSINESS_SEEDS.map((row) => ({
      id: row.sourceId,
      name: row.sourceId,
      baseUrl: row.url,
      enabled: true,
      meta: { fallback: true },
    })),
    mode: "fallback",
  };
}

export async function enqueueSeedBatch(pg, redis, seedPlan, options = {}) {
  const targets = Array.isArray(seedPlan?.targets) ? seedPlan.targets : [];
  if (targets.length === 0) {
    throw new Error("seed targets are empty");
  }

  if (Array.isArray(seedPlan?.sourceSites) && seedPlan.sourceSites.length > 0) {
    await upsertSourceSites(pg, seedPlan.sourceSites);
  }

  const jobId = createId("job");
  const uniqueSourceIds = [...new Set(targets.map((item) => item.sourceId).filter(Boolean))];
  const jobSourceId = uniqueSourceIds.length === 1 ? uniqueSourceIds[0] : "multi-source";

  await pg.query(
    `INSERT INTO crawl_jobs(id, source_id, status, created_at, updated_at)
     VALUES($1, $2, $3, NOW(), NOW())`,
    [jobId, jobSourceId, "seeding"]
  );

  for (const target of targets) {
    const taskId = createId("task");
    const traceId = createId("trace");

    await pg.query(
      `INSERT INTO crawl_tasks(
          id, job_id, trace_id, source_id, url, stage, status, created_at, updated_at
       ) VALUES($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, NOW(), NOW())`,
      [taskId, jobId, traceId, target.sourceId, target.url, "seeded", "queued_fetch"]
    );

    await pg.query(
      `INSERT INTO seed_state(seed_url, source_id, last_enqueued_at, enqueued_count, updated_at)
       VALUES($1, $2, NOW(), 1, NOW())
       ON CONFLICT(seed_url)
       DO UPDATE SET
         source_id = EXCLUDED.source_id,
         last_enqueued_at = NOW(),
         enqueued_count = seed_state.enqueued_count + 1,
         updated_at = NOW()`,
      [target.url, target.sourceId]
    );

    const queuePayload = {
      traceId,
      jobId,
      taskId,
      sourceId: target.sourceId,
      url: target.url,
    };
    await pushQueue(redis, options.queues?.fetch ?? PIPELINE_QUEUES.fetch, queuePayload);
    await recordPipelineEvent(pg, {
      traceId,
      jobId,
      taskId,
      worker: options.workerName ?? "seed",
      name: "task_seeded",
      payload: {
        queue: options.queues?.fetch ?? PIPELINE_QUEUES.fetch,
        url: target.url,
        sourceId: target.sourceId,
        requestedBy: options.requestedBy ?? "system",
        reason: options.reason ?? "seed",
      },
    });
  }

  await pg.query("UPDATE crawl_jobs SET status = $2, updated_at = NOW() WHERE id = $1", [jobId, "queued"]);

  return {
    jobId,
    seedCount: targets.length,
    sourceIds: uniqueSourceIds,
    mode: seedPlan.mode ?? "unknown",
  };
}

export function log(serviceName, level, message, meta = {}) {
  const row = {
    ts: nowIso(),
    service: serviceName,
    level,
    message,
    ...meta,
  };
  process.stdout.write(`${JSON.stringify(row)}\n`);
}

export function sleep(ms) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

export function parseBool(value, fallback = false) {
  if (value === undefined || value === null) return fallback;
  const normalized = String(value).trim().toLowerCase();
  if (["1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"].includes(normalized)) return true;
  if (["0", "false", "no", "n", "off"].includes(normalized)) return false;
  return fallback;
}

function splitCsv(value) {
  if (!value) return [];
  return String(value)
    .split(",")
    .map((item) => item.trim())
    .filter(Boolean);
}

async function loadSourceSitesFromFile(sourceConfigPath, sourceIds) {
  const configuredSourceIds = sourceIds.length > 0 ? sourceIds : DEFAULT_BUSINESS_SOURCE_IDS;
  const selected = new Set(configuredSourceIds.map((item) => String(item).trim()).filter(Boolean));

  try {
    const absolutePath = path.resolve(sourceConfigPath);
    const raw = await fs.readFile(absolutePath, "utf8");
    const json = JSON.parse(raw);
    const sourceRows = Array.isArray(json?.sources) ? json.sources : [];

    const enabledSources = sourceRows
      .filter((row) => row && row.enabled !== false)
      .filter((row) => selected.size === 0 || selected.has(String(row.id || "").trim()));

    const targets = [];
    const sourceSites = [];
    for (const source of enabledSources) {
      const sid = String(source.id || "").trim();
      if (!sid) continue;
      const startUrls = Array.isArray(source.start_urls) ? source.start_urls : [];
      for (const rawUrl of startUrls) {
        const url = normalizeUrl(rawUrl);
        if (!url) continue;
        targets.push({ sourceId: sid, url });
      }

      sourceSites.push({
        id: sid,
        name: String(source.name || sid),
        baseUrl: normalizeUrl(source.base_url) || `https://${sid}`,
        enabled: source.enabled !== false,
        meta: {
          type: source.type ?? null,
          priority: source.priority ?? null,
          include_patterns: source.include_patterns ?? [],
          exclude_patterns: source.exclude_patterns ?? [],
          source_sites_config_path: absolutePath,
        },
      });
    }

    return {
      targets: dedupeSeedTargets(targets),
      sourceSites,
      mode: "source_sites_config",
    };
  } catch {
    return {
      targets: [],
      sourceSites: [],
      mode: "source_sites_config",
    };
  }
}

function dedupeSeedTargets(targets) {
  const map = new Map();
  for (const target of targets) {
    const sourceId = String(target?.sourceId || "").trim();
    const url = normalizeUrl(target?.url);
    if (!sourceId || !url) continue;
    map.set(`${sourceId}|${url}`, { sourceId, url });
  }
  return [...map.values()];
}

function normalizeUrl(raw) {
  try {
    const url = new URL(String(raw).trim());
    return url.toString();
  } catch {
    return "";
  }
}

async function upsertSourceSites(pg, sourceSites) {
  for (const row of sourceSites) {
    if (!row?.id || !row?.baseUrl) continue;
    await pg.query(
      `INSERT INTO source_sites(id, name, base_url, enabled, meta, updated_at)
       VALUES($1, $2, $3, $4, $5::jsonb, NOW())
       ON CONFLICT(id)
       DO UPDATE SET
         name = EXCLUDED.name,
         base_url = EXCLUDED.base_url,
         enabled = EXCLUDED.enabled,
         meta = EXCLUDED.meta,
         updated_at = NOW()`,
      [row.id, row.name || row.id, row.baseUrl, Boolean(row.enabled), JSON.stringify(row.meta ?? {})]
    );
  }
}

function toInt(value, fallback) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isInteger(n) || n <= 0) return fallback;
  return n;
}

export const DEFAULT_POLICY_VERSION = "plan0-v1";

export function nowIso() {
  return new Date().toISOString();
}

export function createId(prefix) {
  const id = crypto.randomUUID();
  return prefix ? `${prefix}_${id}` : id;
}

export function encodeQueueMessage(payload) {
  return JSON.stringify(payload);
}

export function decodeQueueMessage(raw) {
  if (typeof raw !== "string" || raw.trim().length === 0) {
    throw new Error("Queue payload is empty");
  }
  const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
  if (!parsed || typeof parsed !== "object") {
    throw new Error("Queue payload must be object");
  }
  return parsed;
}

export function requireString(value, name) {
  if (typeof value !== "string" || value.trim().length === 0) {
    throw new Error(`Invalid ${name}`);
  }
  return value.trim();
}

import { DEFAULT_POLICY_VERSION } from "@papaweb/contracts";

export const DEFAULT_POLICY = Object.freeze({
  version: DEFAULT_POLICY_VERSION,
  minQualityScore: 0.6,
  minTitleLength: 6,
  requireSummary: true,
});

export function normalizePolicy(config) {
  const policy = {
    ...DEFAULT_POLICY,
    ...(config && typeof config === "object" ? config : {}),
  };
  policy.minQualityScore = clamp01(policy.minQualityScore);
  policy.minTitleLength = toPositiveInt(policy.minTitleLength, DEFAULT_POLICY.minTitleLength);
  policy.requireSummary = Boolean(policy.requireSummary);
  return policy;
}

export function evaluateQuality(input, policyConfig) {
  const policy = normalizePolicy(policyConfig);
  const title = String(input?.title ?? "").trim();
  const summary = String(input?.summary ?? "").trim();
  const httpStatus = Number(input?.httpStatus ?? 0);

  const reasons = [];
  let score = 0;

  if (httpStatus >= 200 && httpStatus < 400) {
    score += 0.2;
  } else {
    reasons.push("http_status_not_ok");
  }

  if (title.length >= policy.minTitleLength) {
    score += 0.5;
  } else {
    reasons.push("title_too_short");
  }

  if (summary.length >= 16) {
    score += 0.3;
  } else if (policy.requireSummary) {
    reasons.push("summary_missing");
  }

  const normalizedScore = Number(score.toFixed(4));
  const pass = normalizedScore >= policy.minQualityScore && reasons.length === 0;
  return {
    pass,
    score: normalizedScore,
    reasons,
    policyVersion: policy.version,
    threshold: policy.minQualityScore,
  };
}

function toPositiveInt(value, fallback) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isInteger(n) || n <= 0) {
    return fallback;
  }
  return n;
}

function clamp01(value) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return DEFAULT_POLICY.minQualityScore;
  if (n < 0) return 0;
  if (n > 1) return 1;
  return n;
}

    page_title: "Demo Tool",

    h1: "Demo Tool",

    captured_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    raw_file: "raw/source-a/page-1.html",
    http_status: 200,
  };

  await writeFile(rawFile, `${JSON.stringify(rawRow)}\n`, "utf8");

  await execFileAsync(process.execPath, ["src/clean.mjs", "--run-id", runId], {
    cwd: root,
  });

  const previewRaw = await readFile(previewFile, "utf8");
  assert.ok(previewRaw.trim().length > 0, "preview jsonl should not be empty");

  const summary = JSON.parse(await readFile(summaryFile, "utf8"));
  assert.equal(summary.run_id, runId);
  assert.equal(summary.input_rows, 1);
  assert.ok(summary.output_entities >= 1, "should produce at least one entity");

  await rm(rawDir, { recursive: true, force: true });
  await rm(cleanDir, { recursive: true, force: true });
});

import fs from "node:fs/promises";

function parseArgs(argv) {
  const args = {
    runId: null,
  };
  for (let i = 0; i < argv.length; i += 1) {
    const token = argv[i];
    const next = argv[i + 1];
    if (token === "--run-id" && next) {
      args.runId = next;
      i += 1;
    }
  }
  return args;
}

async function ensureDir(dirPath) {
  await fs.mkdir(dirPath, { recursive: true });
}

async function fileExists(filePath) {
  try {
    await fs.access(filePath);
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

function normalizeTitle(input) {
  return (input ?? "")
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/\s+/g, " ")
    .replace(/[^\w\u4e00-\u9fa5 ]/g, "")
    .trim();
}

function normalizePublicUrl(input) {
  if (!input) return "";
  try {
    const url = new URL(String(input).replaceAll("&amp;", "&").trim());
    const dropExact = new Set([
      "utm_source",
      "utm_medium",
      "utm_campaign",
      "utm_term",
      "utm_content",
      "fbclid",
      "gclid",
      "msclkid",
      "yclid",
      "spm",
      "source",
      "from",
      "via",
      "ref",
      "ref_src",
      "referrer",
      "aff",
      "aff_id",
      "aff_sub",
      "aff_sub2",
      "affiliate",
      "partner",
    ]);

    const keep = [];
    for (const [key, value] of url.searchParams.entries()) {
      const k = key.trim().toLowerCase();
      const normalized = k.replace(/^amp;/, "");
      if (dropExact.has(normalized)) continue;
      if (normalized.startsWith("utm_")) continue;
      if (normalized.includes("affiliate")) continue;
      if (normalized.startsWith("aff_")) continue;
      keep.push([key, value]);
    }

    url.search = "";
    for (const [key, value] of keep) {
      url.searchParams.append(key, value);
    }
    url.hash = "";
    if (url.pathname !== "/" && url.pathname.endsWith("/")) {
      url.pathname = url.pathname.replace(/\/+$/, "");
    }
    return url.toString();
  } catch {
    return String(input).trim();
  }
}

function pickOfficialUrl(row) {
  const externalLinks = Array.isArray(row.external_links) ? row.external_links : [];
  const officialHints = Array.isArray(row.official_links_hints) ? row.official_links_hints : [];
  const sourceHost = String(row.source_base_host || "").replace(/^www\./, "");
  const candidates = [...officialHints, ...externalLinks];

  const blacklist = [
    "twitter.com",
    "x.com",
    "facebook.com",
    "linkedin.com",
    "youtube.com",
    "instagram.com",
    "t.me",
    "discord.gg",
    "github.com",
    "qq.com",
    "support.qq.com",
    "wpa.qq.com",
    "qm.qq.com",
    "grsm.io",
    "go2cloud.org",
    "shareasale.com",
    "impact.com",
    "partnerstack.com",
    "linktr.ee",
    "passionfroot.me",
    "beacons.ai",
    "bio.link",
    "campsite.bio",
    "bit.ly",
    "tinyurl.com",
    "hostg.xyz",
    "doubleclick.net",
    "googlesyndication.com",
  ];

  for (const link of candidates) {
    try {
      const host = new URL(link).hostname.replace(/^www\./, "");
      if (sourceHost && (host === sourceHost || host.endsWith(`.${sourceHost}`))) continue;
      if (!blacklist.some((b) => host === b || host.endsWith(`.${b}`))) {
        return link;
      }
    } catch {
      // ignore bad url
    }
  }
  return "";
}

function toDomain(url) {
  try {
    return new URL(url).hostname.replace(/^www\./, "");
  } catch {
    return "";
  }
}

function qualityScore(row) {
  let score = 0;
  if (row.page_title) score += 1;
  if (row.meta_description) score += 1;
  if (row.h1) score += 1;
  if (Array.isArray(row.external_links) && row.external_links.length > 0) score += 1;
  if (row.http_status === 200) score += 1;
  return score;
}

async function readJsonl(filePath) {
  const raw = await fs.readFile(filePath, "utf8");
  return raw
    .split(/\r?\n/)
    .map((line) => line.trim())
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((line) => JSON.parse(line));
}

async function findLatestRunId() {
  const entries = await fs.readdir(RAW_ROOT, { withFileTypes: true });
  const runs = entries
    .filter((entry) => entry.isDirectory())
    .map((entry) => entry.name)
    .sort((a, b) => (a > b ? -1 : 1));
  return runs[0] ?? null;
}

async function appendJsonl(filePath, rows) {
  const body = rows.map((row) => JSON.stringify(row)).join("\n");
  await fs.writeFile(filePath, `${body}\n`, "utf8");
}

async function main() {
  const args = parseArgs(process.argv.slice(2));
  const runId = args.runId ?? (await findLatestRunId());
  if (!runId) throw new Error("鏈壘鍒板彲娓呮礂鐨?run_id銆?);

  const inputPath = path.join(RAW_ROOT, runId, "tool_candidates_raw.jsonl");
  const outDir = path.join(CLEAN_ROOT, runId);
  await ensureDir(outDir);

  if (!(await fileExists(inputPath))) {
    await fs.writeFile(path.join(outDir, "tool_entities_preview.jsonl"), "", "utf8");
    await fs.writeFile(
      path.join(outDir, "summary.json"),
      JSON.stringify(
        {
          run_id: runId,
          input_rows: 0,
          output_entities: 0,
          generated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
          note: "tool_candidates_raw.jsonl 涓嶅瓨鍦紝閫氬父琛ㄧず鏈疆鏃犲彲娓呮礂鍊欓€夋暟鎹€?,
        },
        null,
        2
      ),
      "utf8"
    );
    console.log(`娓呮礂瀹屾垚: run_id=${runId}, input=0, entities=0`);
    console.log(`杈撳嚭鐩綍: ${outDir}`);
    return;
  }

  const rows = await readJsonl(inputPath);
  const dedupMap = new Map();

  for (const row of rows) {
    const officialUrlRaw = pickOfficialUrl(row);
    const officialUrl = normalizePublicUrl(officialUrlRaw);
    const officialDomain = toDomain(officialUrl);
    const normalizedTitle = normalizeTitle(row.page_title || row.h1 || "");
    const key =
      officialDomain ||
      (normalizedTitle
        ? `${normalizedTitle}|${row.source_id}`
        : `${String(row.page_url || "").trim()}|${row.source_id}`);
    const normalized = {
      run_id: row.run_id,
      source_id: row.source_id,
      source_type: row.source_type,
      source_name: row.source_name,
      page_url: row.page_url,
      normalized_title: normalizedTitle,
      page_title: row.page_title,
      meta_description: row.meta_description,
      h1: row.h1,
      official_url_raw: officialUrlRaw,
      official_url_hint: officialUrl,
      official_domain: officialDomain,
      captured_at: row.captured_at,
      raw_file: row.raw_file,
      confidence_hint: qualityScore(row),
    };

    if (!dedupMap.has(key)) {
      dedupMap.set(key, normalized);
      continue;
    }

    const previous = dedupMap.get(key);
    if ((previous?.confidence_hint ?? 0) < normalized.confidence_hint) {
      dedupMap.set(key, normalized);
    }
  }

  const entities = [...dedupMap.values()];
  await appendJsonl(path.join(outDir, "tool_entities_preview.jsonl"), entities);
  await fs.writeFile(
    path.join(outDir, "summary.json"),
    JSON.stringify(
      {
        run_id: runId,
        input_rows: rows.length,
        output_entities: entities.length,
        generated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      },
      null,
      2
    ),
    "utf8"
  );

  console.log(`娓呮礂瀹屾垚: run_id=${runId}, input=${rows.length}, entities=${entities.length}`);
  console.log(`杈撳嚭鐩綍: ${outDir}`);
}

main().catch((err) => {
  console.error(err);
  process.exit(1);
});

function nodeFetch(url, options = {}, redirectCount = 0) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    let target;
    try {
      target = new URL(url);
    } catch (err) {
      reject(err);
      return;
    }
    const lib = target.protocol === "https:" ? https : http;
    const reqOptions = {
      method: options.method ?? "GET",
      headers: options.headers ?? {},
    };

    const req = lib.request(target, reqOptions, (res) => {
      const status = Number(res.statusCode ?? 0);
      const location = res.headers.location;
      const shouldFollowRedirect =
        options.redirect === "follow" &&
        Boolean(location) &&
        [301, 302, 303, 307, 308].includes(status) &&
        redirectCount < 8;

      if (shouldFollowRedirect) {
        res.resume();
        const nextUrl = new URL(String(location), target).toString();
        const nextMethod = status === 303 ? "GET" : reqOptions.method;
        const nextOptions = {
          ...options,
          method: nextMethod,
        };
        if (status === 303) {
          delete nextOptions.body;
        }
        nodeFetch(nextUrl, nextOptions, redirectCount + 1).then(resolve).catch(reject);
        return;
      }

      const chunks = [];
      res.on("data", (chunk) => chunks.push(Buffer.from(chunk)));
      res.on("error", reject);
      res.on("end", () => {
        const body = Buffer.concat(chunks);
        const headersObj = {
          get(name) {
            const value = res.headers[String(name).toLowerCase()];
            if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.join(", ");
            if (value === undefined || value === null) return null;
            return String(value);
          },
          getSetCookie() {
            const value = res.headers["set-cookie"];
            if (!value) return [];
            return Array.isArray(value) ? value.map((v) => String(v)) : [String(value)];
          },
        };
        resolve({
          ok: status >= 200 && status < 300,
          status,
          url: target.toString(),
          headers: headersObj,
          arrayBuffer: async () =>
            body.buffer.slice(body.byteOffset, body.byteOffset + body.byteLength),
          text: async () => body.toString("utf8"),
        });
      });
    });

    req.on("error", reject);

    const abortHandler = () => {
      req.destroy(new Error("This operation was aborted"));
    };
    if (options.signal) {
      if (options.signal.aborted) {
        abortHandler();
        return;
      }
      options.signal.addEventListener("abort", abortHandler, { once: true });
    }

    if (options.body !== undefined && options.body !== null) {
      req.write(options.body);
    }
    req.end();
  });
}
