function parseArgs(argv) {
  const args = {
    once: false,
    loop: false,
    sourceIds: null,
    maxUrlsPerSource: null,
    intervalMinutes: DEFAULTS.intervalMinutes,
    timeoutMs: DEFAULTS.timeoutMs,
    retries: DEFAULTS.retries,
    revisitHours: DEFAULTS.revisitHours,
    config: DEFAULTS.config,
    pinchtabUrl: DEFAULTS.pinchtabUrl,
    pinchtabMode: DEFAULTS.pinchtabMode,
    pinchtabTimeoutMs: DEFAULTS.pinchtabTimeoutMs,
    pinchtabWaitMs: DEFAULTS.pinchtabWaitMs,
    pinchtabStatuses: DEFAULTS.pinchtabStatuses,
    pinchtabToken: DEFAULTS.pinchtabToken,
    delayMinMs: DEFAULTS.delayMinMs,
    delayMaxMs: DEFAULTS.delayMaxMs,
    maxFailures: DEFAULTS.maxFailures,
    maxConsecutiveFailures: DEFAULTS.maxConsecutiveFailures,
    sourceConcurrency: 1,
  };

  for (let i = 0; i < argv.length; i += 1) {
    const token = argv[i];
    const next = argv[i + 1];
    if (token === "--once") args.once = true;
    if (token === "--loop") args.loop = true;
    if (token === "--source" && next) {
      args.sourceIds = next.split(",").map((v) => v.trim()).filter(Boolean);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--max-urls-per-source" && next) {
      args.maxUrlsPerSource = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--interval-minutes" && next) {
      args.intervalMinutes = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--timeout-ms" && next) {
      args.timeoutMs = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--retries" && next) {
      args.retries = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--revisit-hours" && next) {
      args.revisitHours = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--config" && next) {
      args.config = path.resolve(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--pinchtab-url" && next) {
      args.pinchtabUrl = next.trim();
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--pinchtab-mode" && next) {
      args.pinchtabMode = next.trim().toLowerCase();
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--pinchtab-timeout-ms" && next) {
      args.pinchtabTimeoutMs = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--pinchtab-wait-ms" && next) {
      args.pinchtabWaitMs = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--pinchtab-statuses" && next) {
      args.pinchtabStatuses = next
        .split(",")
        .map((v) => Number(v.trim()))
        .filter((v) => Number.isInteger(v) && v > 0);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--pinchtab-token" && next) {
      args.pinchtabToken = next.trim();
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--delay-min-ms" && next) {
      args.delayMinMs = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--delay-max-ms" && next) {
      args.delayMaxMs = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--max-failures" && next) {
      args.maxFailures = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--max-consecutive-failures" && next) {
      args.maxConsecutiveFailures = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--source-concurrency" && next) {
      args.sourceConcurrency = Number(next);
      i += 1;
    }
    if (token === "--disable-pinchtab") {
      args.pinchtabUrl = "";
      args.pinchtabMode = "disable";
    }
  }

  if (!args.once && !args.loop) {
    args.once = true;
  }
  if (!["fallback", "always", "disable"].includes(args.pinchtabMode)) {
    args.pinchtabMode = "fallback";
  }
  if (!Number.isFinite(args.sourceConcurrency) || args.sourceConcurrency < 1) {
    args.sourceConcurrency = 1;
  }
  return args;
}

function nowIso() {
  return new Date().toISOString();
}

function runIdFromDate(date = new Date()) {
  return date.toISOString().replaceAll(":", "-").replaceAll(".", "-");
}

function sha1(input) {
  return crypto.createHash("sha1").update(input).digest("hex");
}

async function ensureDir(dirPath) {
  await fs.mkdir(dirPath, { recursive: true });
}

async function fileExists(filePath) {
  try {
    await fs.access(filePath);
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

async function readJson(filePath, fallback = null) {
  if (!(await fileExists(filePath))) return fallback;
  const text = await fs.readFile(filePath, "utf8");
  return JSON.parse(text);
}

async function writeJson(filePath, data) {
  await ensureDir(path.dirname(filePath));
  await fs.writeFile(filePath, JSON.stringify(data, null, 2), "utf8");
}

const appendQueues = new Map();

async function appendJsonl(filePath, row) {
  await ensureDir(path.dirname(filePath));
  const payload = `${JSON.stringify(row)}\n`;
  const prior = appendQueues.get(filePath) || Promise.resolve();
  const next = prior
    .catch(() => {})
    .then(() => fs.appendFile(filePath, payload, "utf8"));
  appendQueues.set(filePath, next);
  await next;
}

function parseSeedLines(text) {
  if (!text) return [];
  const lines = text.split(/\r?\n/);
  const urls = [];
  for (const line of lines) {
    const trimmed = line.trim();
    if (!trimmed) continue;
    if (trimmed.startsWith("#")) continue;
    if (trimmed.startsWith("//")) continue;
    urls.push(trimmed);
  }
  return urls;
}

async function loadManualSeeds(files, baseDir) {
  if (!Array.isArray(files) || files.length === 0) return [];
  const seeds = [];
  for (const file of files) {
    if (!file) continue;
    const filePath = path.isAbsolute(file) ? file : path.resolve(baseDir, file);
    try {
      const text = await fs.readFile(filePath, "utf8");
      seeds.push(...parseSeedLines(text));
    } catch {
      // ignore missing manual seed files
    }
  }
  return [...new Set(seeds)];
}

function sleep(ms) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

function toPositiveInt(value) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return null;
  if (!Number.isInteger(n)) return null;
  if (n <= 0) return null;
  return n;
}

function toPositiveNumber(value) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return null;
  if (n <= 0) return null;
  return n;
}

function normalizeDelayBounds(minValue, maxValue) {
  const min = Number.isFinite(minValue) ? minValue : null;
  const max = Number.isFinite(maxValue) ? maxValue : null;
  if (min === null && max === null) return null;
  if (min === null) return { min: max, max };
  if (max === null) return { min, max: min };
  if (max < min) return { min: max, max: min };
  return { min, max };
}

function randomBetween(minValue, maxValue) {
  const min = Math.floor(minValue);
  const max = Math.floor(maxValue);
  if (!Number.isFinite(min) || !Number.isFinite(max)) return Math.floor(minValue);
  if (max <= min) return min;
  return Math.floor(min + Math.random() * (max - min + 1));
}

function createTimeoutSignal(timeoutMs) {
  const ctrl = new AbortController();
  const timer = setTimeout(() => ctrl.abort(), timeoutMs);
  return {
    signal: ctrl.signal,
    clear: () => clearTimeout(timer),
  };
}

async function readJsonResponse(res) {
  if (!res) return null;
  try {
    if (typeof res.json === "function") {
      return await res.json();
    }
    if (typeof res.text === "function") {
      const raw = await res.text();
      return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null;
    }
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
  return null;
}

function cleanText(text) {
  return text.replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim();
}

function escapeHtml(input) {
  return String(input ?? "")
    .replaceAll("&", "&amp;")
    .replaceAll("<", "&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">", "&gt;")
    .replaceAll("\"", "&quot;")
    .replaceAll("'", "&#39;");
}

function htmlDecode(input) {
  return input
    .replaceAll("&amp;", "&")
    .replaceAll("&lt;", "<")
    .replaceAll("&gt;", ">")
    .replaceAll("&quot;", "\"")
    .replaceAll("&#39;", "'");
}

function normalizePublicUrl(input) {
  try {
    const url = new URL(input);
    const dropParams = [
      "utm_source",
      "utm_medium",
      "utm_campaign",
      "utm_term",
      "utm_content",
      "fbclid",
      "gclid",
    ];
    for (const key of dropParams) {
      url.searchParams.delete(key);
    }
    url.hash = "";
    return url.toString();
  } catch {
    return input;
  }
}

function buildCookieHeader(cookieJar) {
  const entries = Object.entries(cookieJar ?? {}).filter(([, value]) => String(value || "").length > 0);
  return entries.map(([name, value]) => `${name}=${value}`).join("; ");
}

function applySetCookies(setCookieHeaders, cookieJar) {
  if (!cookieJar || !Array.isArray(setCookieHeaders)) return;
  for (const header of setCookieHeaders) {
    if (!header) continue;
    const firstPair = String(header).split(";")[0];
    const idx = firstPair.indexOf("=");
    if (idx <= 0) continue;
    const name = firstPair.slice(0, idx).trim();
    const value = firstPair.slice(idx + 1).trim();
    if (!name) continue;
    cookieJar[name] = value;
  }
}

function normalizeCharsetLabel(label) {
  const value = String(label || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!value) return "utf-8";
  if (value === "utf8") return "utf-8";
  if (value === "gbk" || value === "gb2312") return "gb18030";
  return value;
}

function detectCharsetFromContentType(contentType) {
  const m = String(contentType || "").match(/charset=([^;]+)/i);
  return normalizeCharsetLabel(m?.[1] ?? "");
}

function detectCharsetFromHtmlBytes(bytes) {
  const head = Buffer.from(bytes).toString("latin1", 0, Math.min(bytes.length, 4096));
  const metaCharset = head.match(/<meta[^>]*charset=["']?([\w-]+)["']?/i)?.[1];
  if (metaCharset) return normalizeCharsetLabel(metaCharset);
  const metaHttpEquiv = head.match(
    /<meta[^>]*content=["'][^"']*charset=([^"';\s]+)[^"']*["'][^>]*>/i
  )?.[1];
  return normalizeCharsetLabel(metaHttpEquiv ?? "");
}

function decodeBytes(bytes, contentType) {
  const charsetCandidates = [
    detectCharsetFromContentType(contentType),
    detectCharsetFromHtmlBytes(bytes),
    "utf-8",
  ];
  for (const charset of charsetCandidates) {
    try {
      const text = new TextDecoder(charset).decode(bytes);
      if (text) return { text, charset };
    } catch {
      // try next charset
    }
  }
  return { text: Buffer.from(bytes).toString("utf8"), charset: "utf-8" };
}

function firstMatch(text, regex) {
  const m = text.match(regex);
  if (!m || !m[1]) return "";
  return cleanText(htmlDecode(m[1]).replace(/<[^>]+>/g, " "));
}

function stripHtml(html) {
  return cleanText(
    html
      .replace(/<script[\s\S]*?<\/script>/gi, " ")
      .replace(/<style[\s\S]*?<\/style>/gi, " ")
      .replace(/<[^>]+>/g, " ")
  );
}

function extractAnchors(html, pageUrl) {
  const anchors = [];
  const seen = new Set();
  const regex = /<a\b([^>]*)href=["']([^"']+)["']([^>]*)>([\s\S]*?)<\/a>/gi;
  let match = regex.exec(html);
  while (match) {
    try {
      const rawHref = htmlDecode(match[2]);
      const href = new URL(rawHref, pageUrl).toString();
      const text = cleanText(stripHtml(match[4] || "")).slice(0, 120);
      if (!href.startsWith("http")) {
        match = regex.exec(html);
        continue;
      }
      const key = `${href}|${text}`;
      if (!seen.has(key)) {
        seen.add(key);
        anchors.push({ href, text });
      }
    } catch {
      // ignore bad url
    }
    match = regex.exec(html);
  }
  return anchors;
}

function extractOfficialLinkHints(anchors, sourceHost) {
  const hints = [];
  const seen = new Set();
  const textHint = /(official|website|visit|open app|try|use now|\\u5b98\\u7f51|\\u8bbf\\u95ee|\\u8fdb\\u5165|\\u7acb\\u5373\\u4f53\\u9a8c|\\u4ea7\\u54c1\\u9875?)/i;
  const skipHint = /(privacy|terms|cookie|contact|about|twitter|x\.com|facebook|linkedin|youtube|tiktok|instagram|discord|telegram)/i;

  const pushHint = (url) => {
    const normalized = normalizePublicUrl(url);
    if (!normalized || seen.has(normalized)) return;
    seen.add(normalized);
    hints.push(normalized);
  };

  for (const anchor of anchors) {
    try {
      const url = new URL(anchor.href);
      const host = url.hostname;
      if (host === sourceHost) {
        if (url.pathname.startsWith("/go")) {
          const target =
            url.searchParams.get("url") ||
            url.searchParams.get("target") ||
            url.searchParams.get("u") ||
            "";
          if (target.startsWith("http")) {
            pushHint(target);
          } else if (target) {
            try {
              const decoded = Buffer.from(target, "base64").toString("utf8");
              if (decoded.startsWith("http")) pushHint(decoded);
            } catch {
              // ignore invalid base64
            }
          }
        }
        continue;
      }
      const text = anchor.text || "";
      const lower = `${host}${url.pathname}`.toLowerCase();
      if (skipHint.test(lower)) continue;
      if (textHint.test(text)) pushHint(anchor.href);
    } catch {
      // ignore bad url
    }
  }

  return hints.slice(0, 10);
}

function extractHtmlFacts(html, pageUrl, sourceHost) {
  const title = firstMatch(html, /<title[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/title>/i);
  const metaTag =
    html.match(/<meta[^>]*name=["']description["'][^>]*>/i)?.[0] ??
    html.match(/<meta[^>]*property=["']og:description["'][^>]*>/i)?.[0] ??
    "";
  const metaDescription = firstMatch(metaTag, /content=["']([\s\S]*?)["']/i);
  const h1 = firstMatch(html, /<h1[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/h1>/i);
  const text = stripHtml(html);
  const snippet = text.slice(0, 280);
  const anchors = extractAnchors(html, pageUrl);
  const links = anchors.map((a) => a.href);
  const externalLinks = links
    .filter((link) => {
      try {
        return new URL(link).hostname !== sourceHost;
      } catch {
        return false;
      }
    })
    .map((link) => normalizePublicUrl(link))
    .slice(0, 10);
  const officialHints = extractOfficialLinkHints(anchors, sourceHost);

  return {
    page_title: title,
    meta_description: metaDescription,
    h1,
    text_snippet: snippet,
    external_links: externalLinks,
    official_links_hints: officialHints,
  };
}

function toRegexOrNull(pattern) {
  try {
    return new RegExp(pattern, "i");
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

function matchesAny(url, patterns = []) {
  if (!patterns || patterns.length === 0) return true;
  return patterns.some((pattern) => {
    const rx = toRegexOrNull(pattern);
    if (rx) return rx.test(url);
    return url.toLowerCase().includes(String(pattern).toLowerCase());
  });
}

function shouldCollect(url, source) {
  try {
    const target = new URL(url);
    const base = new URL(source.base_url);
    if (target.hostname !== base.hostname) return false;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }

  if (!matchesAny(url, source.include_patterns ?? [])) return false;
  if (matchesAny(url, source.exclude_patterns ?? []) && (source.exclude_patterns ?? []).length > 0) {
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}

function parseRobots(text, userAgent = "*") {
  const sitemaps = [];
  const groups = [];
  let current = {
    userAgents: [],
    disallowRules: [],
    allowRules: [],
    crawlDelay: null,
  };

  const flushGroup = () => {
    if (current.userAgents.length > 0) {
      groups.push(current);
    }
    current = {
      userAgents: [],
      disallowRules: [],
      allowRules: [],
      crawlDelay: null,
    };
  };

  const lines = text.split(/\r?\n/);
  for (const rawLine of lines) {
    const line = rawLine.split("#")[0].trim();
    if (!line) continue;
    const idx = line.indexOf(":");
    if (idx < 0) continue;
    const key = line.slice(0, idx).trim().toLowerCase();
    const value = line.slice(idx + 1).trim();

    if (key === "sitemap") {
      if (value) sitemaps.push(value);
      continue;
    }
    if (key === "user-agent") {
      if (
        current.userAgents.length > 0 &&
        (current.disallowRules.length > 0 || current.allowRules.length > 0 || current.crawlDelay !== null)
      ) {
        flushGroup();
      }
      if (value) current.userAgents.push(value.toLowerCase());
      continue;
    }
    if (current.userAgents.length === 0) continue;
    if (key === "disallow") current.disallowRules.push(value);
    if (key === "allow") current.allowRules.push(valu…1038 tokens truncated…    baseUrl,
        tabId,
        "(() => ({ html: document.documentElement.outerHTML, url: location.href, title: document.title }))()",
        timeoutMs,
        token
      );
      if (evalRes.ok) {
        const result = evalRes.data?.result ?? null;
        if (result && typeof result.html === "string" && result.html.trim().length > 0) {
          evalPayload = {
            html: result.html,
            url: cleanText(result.url || openData?.url || url),
            status: evalRes.status,
          };
        }
      }
    } catch {
      evalPayload = null;
    }

    if (evalPayload?.html) {
      return {
        ok: true,
        status: evalPayload.status ?? 200,
        finalUrl: evalPayload.url,
        text: evalPayload.html,
        durationMs: Date.now() - started,
        contentType: "text/html; charset=utf-8",
        contentLength: Buffer.byteLength(evalPayload.html, "utf8"),
        decodedCharset: "utf-8",
        error: null,
        fetchChannel: "pinchtab",
      };
    }

    const textCtrl = createTimeoutSignal(timeoutMs);
    const textRes = await fetchCompat(
      `${baseUrl.replace(/\/+$/, "")}/text?tabId=${encodeURIComponent(tabId)}`,
      {
        method: "GET",
        headers: {
          ...pinchtabAuthHeaders(token),
        },
        signal: textCtrl.signal,
      }
    );
    textCtrl.clear();
    const textRaw = await textRes.text();
    let parsed;
    try {
      parsed = JSON.parse(textRaw);
    } catch {
      parsed = null;
    }

    const renderedTitle = cleanText(parsed?.title || "");
    const renderedText = cleanText(parsed?.text || "");
    const finalUrl = cleanText(parsed?.url || openData?.url || url);
    const pseudoHtml = buildPseudoHtmlFromText(renderedTitle, renderedText);

    return {
      ok: textRes.ok,
      status: textRes.status,
      finalUrl,
      text: pseudoHtml,
      durationMs: Date.now() - started,
      contentType: "text/html; charset=utf-8",
      contentLength: Buffer.byteLength(pseudoHtml, "utf8"),
      decodedCharset: "utf-8",
      error: textRes.ok ? null : `pinchtab text failed: ${textRes.status}`,
      fetchChannel: "pinchtab",
    };
  } catch (err) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      status: 0,
      finalUrl: url,
      text: "",
      durationMs: Date.now() - started,
      contentType: "",
      contentLength: 0,
      decodedCharset: "",
      error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
      fetchChannel: "pinchtab",
    };
  } finally {
    if (tabId) {
      try {
        const closeCtrl = createTimeoutSignal(5000);
        await fetchCompat(`${baseUrl.replace(/\/+$/, "")}/tab`, {
          method: "POST",
          headers: {
            "content-type": "application/json",
            ...pinchtabAuthHeaders(token),
          },
          body: JSON.stringify({ action: "close", tabId }),
          signal: closeCtrl.signal,
        });
        closeCtrl.clear();
      } catch {
        // ignore close failure
      }
    }
  }
}

async function fetchText(url, options) {
  const { timeoutMs, retries, headers, cookieJar, pinchtab } = options;
  let lastError = null;
  let pinchtabTried = false;
  const pinchtabMode = pinchtab?.mode ?? "fallback";

  if (pinchtabMode === "always" && pinchtab?.baseUrl) {
    const primary = await fetchTextViaPinchtab(url, {
      baseUrl: pinchtab.baseUrl,
      timeoutMs: pinchtab.timeoutMs ?? timeoutMs,
      waitMs: pinchtab.waitMs ?? 1000,
      token: pinchtab.token,
      headers,
    });
    return primary;
  }

  for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= retries; attempt += 1) {
    const started = Date.now();
    const ctrl = new AbortController();
    const timer = setTimeout(() => ctrl.abort(), timeoutMs);
    try {
      const requestHeaders = { ...(headers ?? {}) };
      const cookieHeader = buildCookieHeader(cookieJar);
      if (cookieHeader) requestHeaders.Cookie = cookieHeader;
      const res = await fetchCompat(url, {
        method: "GET",
        redirect: "follow",
        headers: requestHeaders,
        signal: ctrl.signal,
      });
      const contentType = res.headers.get("content-type") ?? "";
      const bytes = new Uint8Array(await res.arrayBuffer());
      const decoded = decodeBytes(bytes, contentType);
      const setCookieHeaders =
        (typeof res.headers.getSetCookie === "function" ? res.headers.getSetCookie() : null) ??
        (res.headers.get("set-cookie") ? [res.headers.get("set-cookie")] : []);
      applySetCookies(setCookieHeaders, cookieJar);
      clearTimeout(timer);
      const pinchtabEnabled = Boolean(pinchtab?.baseUrl);
      const shouldFallbackToPinchtab =
        pinchtabEnabled &&
        !pinchtabTried &&
        !res.ok &&
        (pinchtab?.statuses ?? []).includes(res.status);
      if (shouldFallbackToPinchtab) {
        pinchtabTried = true;
        const fallback = await fetchTextViaPinchtab(url, {
          baseUrl: pinchtab.baseUrl,
          timeoutMs: pinchtab.timeoutMs ?? timeoutMs,
          waitMs: pinchtab.waitMs ?? 1000,
          token: pinchtab.token,
          headers,
        });
        if (fallback?.ok) {
          return fallback;
        }
      }

      return {
        ok: res.ok,
        status: res.status,
        finalUrl: res.url,
        text: decoded.text,
        durationMs: Date.now() - started,
        contentType,
        contentLength: Number(res.headers.get("content-length") ?? bytes.byteLength),
        decodedCharset: decoded.charset,
        error: null,
        fetchChannel: "http",
      };
    } catch (err) {
      clearTimeout(timer);
      lastError = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);

      const pinchtabEnabled = Boolean(pinchtab?.baseUrl);
      if (pinchtabEnabled && !pinchtabTried && attempt >= retries) {
        pinchtabTried = true;
        const fallback = await fetchTextViaPinchtab(url, {
          baseUrl: pinchtab.baseUrl,
          timeoutMs: pinchtab.timeoutMs ?? timeoutMs,
          waitMs: pinchtab.waitMs ?? 1000,
          token: pinchtab.token,
          headers,
        });
        if (fallback?.ok) {
          return fallback;
        }
      }
      if (attempt < retries) {
        await sleep((attempt + 1) * 1200);
      }
    }
  }

  return {
    ok: false,
    status: 0,
    finalUrl: url,
    text: "",
    durationMs: 0,
    contentType: "",
    contentLength: 0,
    decodedCharset: "",
    error: lastError ?? "unknown fetch error",
    fetchChannel: "http",
  };
}

function recentlyFetched(state, urlHash, revisitHours) {
  const row = state.urls[urlHash];
  if (!row || !row.last_fetched_at) return false;
  const deltaMs = Date.now() - new Date(row.last_fetched_at).getTime();
  return deltaMs < revisitHours * 3600 * 1000;
}

async function runSource(source, context) {
  const {
    runId,
    args,
    headers,
    state,
    candidatesPath,
    tracePath,
    jobsPath,
    pagesDir,
  } = context;

  const sourceHost = new URL(source.base_url).hostname;
  const cookieJar = {};
  const pinchtabModeRaw = String(source.pinchtab_mode ?? args.pinchtabMode ?? "fallback").toLowerCase();
  const pinchtabMode = ["fallback", "always", "disable"].includes(pinchtabModeRaw)
    ? pinchtabModeRaw
    : "fallback";
  const pinchtabConfig =
    source.render_via_pinchtab && args.pinchtabUrl && pinchtabMode !== "disable"
      ? {
          baseUrl: args.pinchtabUrl,
          timeoutMs: args.pinchtabTimeoutMs,
          waitMs: args.pinchtabWaitMs,
          statuses: args.pinchtabStatuses,
          token: args.pinchtabToken,
          mode: pinchtabMode,
        }
      : null;
  const robotsUrl = `${source.base_url.replace(/\/+$/, "")}/robots.txt`;
  const sourceSummary = {
    run_id: runId,
    source_id: source.id,
    source_name: source.name,
    source_type: source.type,
    base_url: source.base_url,
    robots_url: robotsUrl,
    robots_status: 0,
    crawl_delay_seconds: null,
    disallow_all: false,
    manual_seed_count: 0,
    candidate_url_count: 0,
    fetched_url_count: 0,
    failed_url_count: 0,
    skipped_recent_count: 0,
    captured_at: nowIso(),
  };

  const robotsRes = await fetchText(robotsUrl, {
    timeoutMs: args.timeoutMs,
    retries: args.retries,
    headers,
    cookieJar,
  });
  sourceSummary.robots_status = robotsRes.status;
  const headerUserAgent = headers["User-Agent"] || headers["user-agent"] || "";
  const robotsMeta = parseRobots(robotsRes.text || "", headerUserAgent);
  sourceSummary.crawl_delay_seconds = robotsMeta.crawlDelay;
  sourceSummary.disallow_all = robotsMeta.disallowAll;
  if (robotsMeta.disallowAll) {
    await appendJsonl(jobsPath, sourceSummary);
    return sourceSummary;
  }

  const sitemapQueue = [...(robotsMeta.sitemaps ?? [])];
  const seenSitemaps = new Set();
  const maxSitemaps = source.max_sitemaps ?? 1;

  const discovered = new Set(source.start_urls ?? []);
  const manualSeeds = await loadManualSeeds(source.manual_seed_files ?? [], CRAWLER_ROOT);
  for (const seed of manualSeeds) {
    discovered.add(seed);
  }
  sourceSummary.manual_seed_count = manualSeeds.length;
  while (sitemapQueue.length > 0 && seenSitemaps.size < maxSitemaps) {
    const sitemapUrl = sitemapQueue.shift();
    if (!sitemapUrl || seenSitemaps.has(sitemapUrl)) continue;
    seenSitemaps.add(sitemapUrl);
    if (shouldStop) break;
    const sitemapRes = await fetchText(sitemapUrl, {
      timeoutMs: args.timeoutMs,
      retries: args.retries,
      headers,
      cookieJar,
    });
    await appendJsonl(tracePath, {
      trace_id: sha1(`${runId}|${source.id}|${sitemapUrl}`),
      run_id: runId,
      source_id: source.id,
      request_url: sitemapUrl,
      final_url: sitemapRes.finalUrl,
      http_status: sitemapRes.status,
      duration_ms: sitemapRes.durationMs,
      content_type: sitemapRes.contentType,
      content_length: sitemapRes.contentLength,
      fetch_channel: sitemapRes.fetchChannel ?? "http",
      fetched_at: nowIso(),
      error: sitemapRes.error,
    });

    const locs = parseSitemapLocs(sitemapRes.text);
    for (const loc of locs) {
      const normalized = loc.toLowerCase();
      if (normalized.endsWith(".xml") || normalized.includes("sitemap")) {
        if (!seenSitemaps.has(loc) && sitemapQueue.length + seenSitemaps.size < maxSitemaps * 4) {
          sitemapQueue.push(loc);
        }
        continue;
      }
      if (shouldCollect(loc, source)) discovered.add(loc);
    }
  }

  // Fetch start URLs to discover detail links.
  for (const seedUrl of source.start_urls ?? []) {
    if (shouldStop) break;
    const seedRes = await fetchText(seedUrl, {
      timeoutMs: args.timeoutMs,
      retries: args.retries,
      headers,
      cookieJar,
      pinchtab: pinchtabConfig,
    });
    await appendJsonl(tracePath, {
      trace_id: sha1(`${runId}|${source.id}|seed|${seedUrl}`),
      run_id: runId,
      source_id: source.id,
      request_url: seedUrl,
      final_url: seedRes.finalUrl,
      http_status: seedRes.status,
      duration_ms: seedRes.durationMs,
      content_type: seedRes.contentType,
      content_length: seedRes.contentLength,
      fetch_channel: seedRes.fetchChannel ?? "http",
      fetched_at: nowIso(),
      error: seedRes.error,
    });
    if (!seedRes.ok || !seedRes.contentType.toLowerCase().includes("html")) continue;
    const anchors = extractAnchors(seedRes.text, seedUrl);
    for (const anchor of anchors) {
      if (shouldCollect(anchor.href, source)) discovered.add(anchor.href);
    }
  }

  let candidateUrls = [...discovered].filter((url) => shouldCollect(url, source));
  const maxUrls = args.maxUrlsPerSource ?? source.max_candidate_urls ?? 100;
  if (candidateUrls.length > maxUrls) {
    candidateUrls = candidateUrls.slice(0, maxUrls);
  }
  sourceSummary.candidate_url_count = candidateUrls.length;

  const robotsDelayMs = robotsMeta.crawlDelay ? robotsMeta.crawlDelay * 1000 : 0;
  const baseDelayMs = Math.max(source.delay_ms ?? 1500, robotsDelayMs);
  const delayBounds = normalizeDelayBounds(
    toPositiveNumber(args.delayMinMs) ?? toPositiveNumber(source.delay_min_ms) ?? baseDelayMs,
    toPositiveNumber(args.delayMaxMs) ?? toPositiveNumber(source.delay_max_ms) ?? baseDelayMs
  );
  let delayMinMs = baseDelayMs;
  let delayMaxMs = baseDelayMs;
  if (delayBounds) {
    delayMinMs = Math.max(delayBounds.min, robotsDelayMs);
    delayMaxMs = Math.max(delayBounds.max, delayMinMs, robotsDelayMs);
  }
  const maxFailures = toPositiveInt(args.maxFailures) ?? toPositiveInt(source.max_failures);
  const maxConsecutiveFailures =
    toPositiveInt(args.maxConsecutiveFailures) ?? toPositiveInt(source.max_consecutive_failures);
  let consecutiveFailures = 0;
  sourceSummary.pinchtab_mode = pinchtabConfig?.mode ?? "disable";
  sourceSummary.delay_min_ms = delayMinMs;
  sourceSummary.delay_max_ms = delayMaxMs;
  sourceSummary.max_failures = maxFailures;
  sourceSummary.max_consecutive_failures = maxConsecutiveFailures;
  sourceSummary.aborted_reason = null;

  for (let i = 0; i < candidateUrls.length; i += 1) {
    if (shouldStop) break;
    const pageUrl = candidateUrls[i];
    const urlHash = sha1(pageUrl);
    if (recentlyFetched(state, urlHash, args.revisitHours)) {
      sourceSummary.skipped_recent_count += 1;
      continue;
    }

    if (i > 0) await sleep(randomBetween(delayMinMs, delayMaxMs));

    const response = await fetchText(pageUrl, {
      timeoutMs: args.timeoutMs,
      retries: args.retries,
      headers,
      cookieJar,
      pinchtab: pinchtabConfig,
    });
    const fetchedAt = nowIso();
    const traceId = sha1(`${runId}|${source.id}|${pageUrl}`);
    await appendJsonl(tracePath, {
      trace_id: traceId,
      run_id: runId,
      source_id: source.id,
      request_url: pageUrl,
      final_url: response.finalUrl,
      http_status: response.status,
      duration_ms: response.durationMs,
      content_type: response.contentType,
      content_length: response.contentLength,
      fetch_channel: response.fetchChannel ?? "http",
      fetched_at: fetchedAt,
      error: response.error,
    });

    const isHtmlOk =
      response.ok && String(response.contentType || "").toLowerCase().includes("html");
    const stateRow = state.urls[urlHash] ?? {
      source_id: source.id,
      url: pageUrl,
      first_seen_at: fetchedAt,
    };
    stateRow.last_status = response.status;
    if (isHtmlOk) {
      stateRow.last_fetched_at = fetchedAt;
    } else {
      stateRow.last_failed_at = fetchedAt;
    }
    state.urls[urlHash] = stateRow;

    if (!isHtmlOk) {
      sourceSummary.failed_url_count += 1;
      consecutiveFailures += 1;
      if (maxFailures && sourceSummary.failed_url_count >= maxFailures) {
        sourceSummary.aborted_reason = `max_failures(${maxFailures})`;
        break;
      }
      if (maxConsecutiveFailures && consecutiveFailures >= maxConsecutiveFailures) {
        sourceSummary.aborted_reason = `max_consecutive_failures(${maxConsecutiveFailures})`;
        break;
      }
      continue;
    }
    consecutiveFailures = 0;

    const html = response.text;
    const fileName = `${source.id}_${String(i + 1).padStart(4, "0")}_${urlHash}.html`;
    const rawFile = path.join(pagesDir, fileName);
    await fs.writeFile(rawFile, html, "utf8");

    const facts = extractHtmlFacts(html, pageUrl, sourceHost);
    const capturedAt = nowIso();
    const candidate = {
      run_id: runId,
      source_id: source.id,
      source_name: source.name,
      source_type: source.type,
      page_url: pageUrl,
      http_status: response.status,
      fetch_channel: response.fetchChannel ?? "http",
      page_title: facts.page_title,
      meta_description: facts.meta_description,
      h1: facts.h1,
      external_links: facts.external_links,
      official_links_hints: facts.official_links_hints,
      text_snippet: facts.text_snippet,
      raw_file: path.relative(CRAWLER_ROOT, rawFile).replaceAll("\\", "/"),
      source_base_host: sourceHost,
      captured_at: capturedAt,
      evidence: [
        { field: "page_title", extractor: "html:title", source_url: pageUrl },
        { field: "meta_description", extractor: "meta[name=description]", source_url: pageUrl },
        { field: "h1", extractor: "html:h1:first", source_url: pageUrl },
        { field: "external_links", extractor: "html:a[href]", source_url: pageUrl },
      ],
    };
    await appendJsonl(candidatesPath, candidate);
    sourceSummary.fetched_url_count += 1;
  }

  await appendJsonl(jobsPath, sourceSummary);
  return sourceSummary;
}

async function runWithConcurrency(items, limit, worker) {
  const results = new Array(items.length);
  let index = 0;
  const executing = new Set();

  const enqueue = async () => {
    if (index >= items.length) return;
    const currentIndex = index;
    const item = items[index];
    index += 1;

    const p = Promise.resolve()
      .then(() => worker(item))
      .then((result) => {
        results[currentIndex] = result;
      })
      .finally(() => {
        executing.delete(p);
      });
    executing.add(p);

    if (executing.size >= limit) {
      await Promise.race(executing);
    }
    return enqueue();
  };

  await enqueue();
  await Promise.all(executing);
  return results;
}

async function runOnce(args) {
  const config = await readJson(args.config, null);
  if (!config || !Array.isArray(config.sources)) {
    throw new Error(`Invalid config file: ${args.config}`);
  }
  const selectedSources = config.sources
    .filter((s) => s.enabled)
    .filter((s) => !args.sourceIds || args.sourceIds.includes(s.id));

  const runId = runIdFromDate();
  const runDir = path.join(RAW_ROOT, runId);
  const pagesDir = path.join(runDir, "pages");
  await ensureDir(pagesDir);
  await ensureDir(STATE_ROOT);

  const candidatesPath = path.join(runDir, "tool_candidates_raw.jsonl");
  const tracePath = path.join(runDir, "download_trace.jsonl");
  const jobsPath = path.join(runDir, "source_site_snapshot.jsonl");
  const statePath = path.join(STATE_ROOT, "seen-urls.v1.json");
  const state = (await readJson(statePath, { version: "v1", urls: {} })) ?? {
    version: "v1",
    urls: {},
  };

  const headers = {
    ...(config.default_headers ?? {}),
  };

  console.log(`[${nowIso()}] Starting crawl run_id=${runId} sources=${selectedSources.length}`);
  const summaries = [];
  const runOne = async (source) => {
    if (shouldStop) return null;
    console.log(`- Processing source=${source.id}`);
    const summary = await runSource(source, {
      runId,
      args,
      headers,
      state,
      candidatesPath,
      tracePath,
      jobsPath,
      pagesDir,
    });
    console.log(
      `  Done source=${source.id}, candidates=${summary.candidate_url_count}, fetched=${summary.fetched_url_count}, failed=${summary.failed_url_count}, skipped_recent=${summary.skipped_recent_count}`
    );
    return summary;
  };

  const concurrency = Math.min(args.sourceConcurrency, selectedSources.length);
  if (concurrency <= 1) {
    for (const source of selectedSources) {
      if (shouldStop) break;
      const summary = await runOne(source);
      if (summary) summaries.push(summary);
    }
  } else {
    const results = await runWithConcurrency(selectedSources, concurrency, runOne);
    for (const summary of results) {
      if (summary) summaries.push(summary);
    }
  }

  await writeJson(statePath, state);
  await writeJson(path.join(runDir, "run-summary.json"), {
    run_id: runId,
    created_at: nowIso(),
    source_count: summaries.length,
    summaries,
  });
  console.log(`[${nowIso()}] run_id=${runId} complete. Output dir: ${runDir}`);
}

async function main() {
  const args = parseArgs(process.argv.slice(2));
  do {
    await runOnce(args);
    if (!args.loop || shouldStop) break;
    const sleepMs = args.intervalMinutes * 60 * 1000;
    console.log(`Entering wait: ${args.intervalMinutes} minutes`);
    await sleep(sleepMs);
  } while (!shouldStop);
}

main().catch((err) => {
  console.error(err);
  process.exit(1);
});

function nodeFetch(url, options = {}, redirectCount = 0) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    let target;
    try {
      target = new URL(url);
    } catch (err) {
      reject(err);
      return;
    }
    const lib = target.protocol === "https:" ? https : http;
    const reqOptions = {
      method: options.method ?? "GET",
      headers: options.headers ?? {},
    };

    const req = lib.request(target, reqOptions, (res) => {
      const status = Number(res.statusCode ?? 0);
      const location = res.headers.location;
      const shouldFollowRedirect =
        options.redirect === "follow" &&
        Boolean(location) &&
        [301, 302, 303, 307, 308].includes(status) &&
        redirectCount < 8;

      if (shouldFollowRedirect) {
        res.resume();
        const nextUrl = new URL(String(location), target).toString();
        const nextMethod = status === 303 ? "GET" : reqOptions.method;
        const nextOptions = {
          ...options,
          method: nextMethod,
        };
        if (status === 303) {
          delete nextOptions.body;
        }
        nodeFetch(nextUrl, nextOptions, redirectCount + 1).then(resolve).catch(reject);
        return;
      }

      const chunks = [];
      res.on("data", (chunk) => chunks.push(Buffer.from(chunk)));
      res.on("error", reject);
      res.on("end", () => {
        const body = Buffer.concat(chunks);
        const headersObj = {
          get(name) {
            const value = res.headers[String(name).toLowerCase()];
            if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.join(", ");
            if (value === undefined || value === null) return null;
            return String(value);
          },
        };
        resolve({
          ok: status >= 200 && status < 300,
          status,
          url: target.toString(),
          headers: headersObj,
          arrayBuffer: async () =>
            body.buffer.slice(body.byteOffset, body.byteOffset + body.byteLength),
          text: async () => body.toString("utf8"),
        });
      });
    });

    req.on("error", reject);

    if (options.body !== undefined && options.body !== null) {
      req.write(options.body);
    }
    req.end();
  });
}

const fetchCompat = typeof globalThis.fetch === "function" ? globalThis.fetch.bind(globalThis) : nodeFetch;

async function readText(filePath) {
  try {
    return await fs.readFile(filePath, "utf8");
  } catch {
    return "";
  }
}

function parseSeedLines(text) {
  if (!text) return [];
  const lines = text.split(/\r?\n/);
  const urls = [];
  for (const line of lines) {
    const trimmed = line.trim();
    if (!trimmed) continue;
    if (trimmed.startsWith("#")) continue;
    if (trimmed.startsWith("//")) continue;
    urls.push(trimmed);
  }
  return urls;
}

function slugify(input) {
  return String(input || "")
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/https?:\/\//g, "")
    .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-")
    .replace(/^-+|-+$/g, "")
    .slice(0, 120) || "page";
}

async function writeSeedFile(outputPath, newUrls) {
  const raw = await readText(outputPath);
  const lines = raw.split(/\r?\n/);
  const header = [];
  const existing = [];
  for (const line of lines) {
    const t = line.trim();
    if (!t) {
      header.push(line);
    } else if (t.startsWith("#")) {
      header.push(line);
    } else {
      existing.push(t);
    }
  }
  const merged = new Map();
  for (const url of existing) merged.set(url.toLowerCase(), url);
  for (const url of newUrls) merged.set(url.toLowerCase(), url);
  const body = Array.from(merged.values()).sort();
  const headerText = header.join("\n").trimEnd();
  const content = `${headerText ? `${headerText}\n` : ""}${body.join("\n")}\n`;
  await fs.mkdir(path.dirname(outputPath), { recursive: true });
  await fs.writeFile(outputPath, content, "utf8");
  return { previous: existing.length, total: body.length };
}

async function appendLog(logPath, row) {
  await fs.mkdir(path.dirname(logPath), { recursive: true });
  await fs.appendFile(logPath, `${JSON.stringify(row)}\n`, "utf8");
}

async function requestJson(url, options) {
  const res = await fetchCompat(url, options);
  const text = await res.text();
  let body = null;
  try {
    body = text ? JSON.parse(text) : null;
  } catch {
    body = null;
  }
  if (!res.ok) {
    const msg = body?.error || body?.message || text || `HTTP ${res.status}`;
    throw new Error(`request failed ${url}: ${msg}`);
  }
  return body;
}

function baseUrl(input) {
  return input.replace(/\/+$/, "");
}

async function openTab(pinchtabBase, url) {
  const body = await requestJson(`${pinchtabBase}/tab`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify({ action: "new", url }),
  });
  return String(body?.tabId || "");
}

async function navigateTab(pinchtabBase, tabId, url) {
  const body = await requestJson(`${pinchtabBase}/tabs/${tabId}/navigate`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify({ url }),
  });
  return body;
}

async function evaluateTab(pinchtabBase, tabId, expression) {
  const body = await requestJson(`${pinchtabBase}/tabs/${tabId}/evaluate`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify({ expression }),
  });
  return body?.result;
}

async function closeTab(pinchtabBase, tabId) {
  await requestJson(`${pinchtabBase}/tabs/${tabId}/close`, {
    method: "POST",
  });
}

async function sleep(ms) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

async function discoverCategories(pinchtabBase, args) {
  const tabId = await openTab(pinchtabBase, args.categoryUrl);
  if (!tabId) throw new Error("failed to open tab for category discovery");
  await sleep(args.categoryPageWaitMs);
  for (let i = 0; i < args.categoryMaxScroll; i += 1) {
    await evaluateTab(pinchtabBase, tabId, "window.scrollBy(0, Math.floor(window.innerHeight * 0.9));");
    await sleep(args.categoryScrollWaitMs);
  }
  const expr = `(() => {
    const out = new Set();
    document.querySelectorAll('a[href^=\"/category/\"]').forEach((a) => {
      try {
        const u = new URL(a.getAttribute('href'), location.href);
        if (!u.hostname.endsWith('toolify.ai')) return;
        if (!u.pathname.startsWith('/category/')) return;
        if (u.pathname.startsWith('/category-attribute/')) return;
        if (u.pathname === '/category') return;
        u.search = '';
        u.hash = '';
        out.add(u.toString());
      } catch (err) {}
    });
    return Array.from(out);
  })()`;
  const links = await evaluateTab(pinchtabBase, tabId, expr);
  await closeTab(pinchtabBase, tabId);
  return Array.isArray(links) ? links.filter(Boolean) : [];
}

async function main() {
  const args = parseArgs(process.argv.slice(2));
  const pinchtabBase = baseUrl(args.pinchtabUrl);
  if (args.discoverCategories) {
    const discovered = await discoverCategories(pinchtabBase, args);
    if (discovered.length > 0) {
      await writeSeedFile(args.input, discovered);
      console.log(`[seed-toolify] discovered categories: ${discovered.length}`);
    } else {
      console.log("[seed-toolify] no categories discovered");
    }
  }
  const inputText = await readText(args.input);
  let categoryUrls = parseSeedLines(inputText);
  if (categoryUrls.length === 0) {
    throw new Error(`no category urls found in ${args.input}`);
  }
  if (args.maxCategories && args.maxCategories > 0 && categoryUrls.length > args.maxCategories) {
    categoryUrls = categoryUrls.slice(0, args.maxCategories);
  }

  const htmlDir = args.htmlDir;
  if (args.saveHtml) {
    await fs.mkdir(htmlDir, { recursive: true });
  }

  let tabId = await openTab(pinchtabBase, categoryUrls[0]);
  if (!tabId) throw new Error("failed to open pinchtab tab");

  const allLinks = new Set();
  const extractExpr = `(() => {
    const out = new Set();
    document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="/tool/"]').forEach((a) => {
      try {
        const u = new URL(a.href, location.href);
        if (!u.hostname.endsWith('toolify.ai')) return;
        if (!u.pathname.startsWith('/tool/')) return;
        u.search = '';
        u.hash = '';
        out.add(u.toString());
      } catch (err) {}
    });
    return Array.from(out);
  })()`;

  for (const url of categoryUrls) {
    await navigateTab(pinchtabBase, tabId, url);
    await sleep(args.pageWaitMs);

    for (let i = 0; i < args.maxScroll; i += 1) {
      await evaluateTab(pinchtabBase, tabId, "window.scrollBy(0, Math.floor(window.innerHeight * 0.9));");
      await sleep(args.scrollWaitMs);
    }

    const links = await evaluateTab(pinchtabBase, tabId, extractExpr);
    const list = Array.isArray(links) ? links.filter(Boolean) : [];
    const before = allLinks.size;
    for (const link of list) allLinks.add(link);
    const added = allLinks.size - before;

    let htmlPath = "";
    if (args.saveHtml) {
      const html = await evaluateTab(pinchtabBase, tabId, "document.documentElement.outerHTML");
      const fileName = `${slugify(url)}-${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, "-")}.html`;
      htmlPath = path.join(htmlDir, fileName);
      await fs.writeFile(htmlPath, html || "", "utf8");
    }

    await appendLog(args.logPath, {
      at: new Date().toISOString(),
      url,
      extracted: list.length,
      added,
      total: allLinks.size,
      html_path: htmlPath || null,
    });

    console.log(`[seed-toolify] ${url} extracted=${list.length} added=${added} total=${allLinks.size}`);
    if (args.targetTotal > 0 && allLinks.size >= args.targetTotal) {
      console.log(`[seed-toolify] target reached: ${allLinks.size}/${args.targetTotal}`);
      break;
    }
  }

  await closeTab(pinchtabBase, tabId);

  const written = await writeSeedFile(args.output, Array.from(allLinks));
  console.log(`[seed-toolify] seed file updated: ${args.output} (total=${written.total})`);
}

main().catch((err) => {
  console.error(err);
  process.exit(1);
});

    }
    if (token === "--max-noise-rate" && next) {
      args.maxNoiseRate = Number(next);
      i += 1;
      continue;
    }
    if (token === "--min-official-fill-rate" && next) {
      args.minOfficialFillRate = Number(next);
      i += 1;
      continue;
    }
  }

  return args;
}

async function ensureDir(dirPath) {
  await fs.mkdir(dirPath, { recursive: true });
}

async function fileExists(filePath) {
  try {
    await fs.access(filePath);
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

async function readJson(filePath) {
  const raw = await fs.readFile(filePath, "utf8");
  return JSON.parse(raw);
}

async function readJsonl(filePath) {
  if (!(await fileExists(filePath))) return [];
  const raw = await fs.readFile(filePath, "utf8");
  return raw
    .split(/\r?\n/)
    .map((line) => line.trim())
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((line) => JSON.parse(line));
}

async function findLatestRunId() {
  const entries = await fs.readdir(RAW_ROOT, { withFileTypes: true });
  const runs = entries
    .filter((entry) => entry.isDirectory())
    .map((entry) => entry.name)
    .sort((a, b) => (a > b ? -1 : 1));
  return runs[0] ?? null;
}

function parseHost(url) {
  try {
    return new URL(url).hostname.replace(/^www\./, "").toLowerCase();
  } catch {
    return "";
  }
}

function sampleRows(rows, sampleSize) {
  if (rows.length <= sampleSize) return rows;
  const picked = [];
  const step = rows.length / sampleSize;
  for (let i = 0; i < sampleSize; i += 1) {
    const idx = Math.min(rows.length - 1, Math.floor(i * step));
    picked.push(rows[idx]);
  }
  return picked;
}

function analyzeOfficialUrl(url, sourceHosts) {
  const reasons = [];
  let host = "";
  try {
    const parsed = new URL(url);
    host = parsed.hostname.replace(/^www\./, "").toLowerCase();
    if (!host) reasons.push("missing_host");

    if ([...sourceHosts].some((s) => host === s || host.endsWith(`.${s}`))) {
      reasons.push("source_domain_link");
    }

    const hostBlacklist = [
      "futurepedia.io",
      "ainav.cn",
      "botlib.cn",
      "twitter.com",
      "x.com",
      "facebook.com",
      "linkedin.com",
      "youtube.com",
      "instagram.com",
      "doubleclick.net",
      "googlesyndication.com",
      "grsm.io",
      "passionfroot.me",
      "beacons.ai",
      "bio.link",
      "campsite.bio",
      "bit.ly",
      "tinyurl.com",
      "linktr.ee",
      "hostg.xyz",
    ];
    if (hostBlacklist.some((d) => host === d || host.endsWith(`.${d}`))) {
      reasons.push("blacklisted_host");
    }

    for (const [key] of parsed.searchParams.entries()) {
      const normalized = key.trim().toLowerCase().replace(/^amp;/, "");
      if (
        normalized.startsWith("utm_") ||
        normalized === "ref" ||
        normalized === "from" ||
        normalized === "source" ||
        normalized === "via" ||
        normalized.startsWith("aff") ||
        normalized.includes("affiliate")
      ) {
        reasons.push("tracking_query");
        break;
      }
    }
  } catch {
    reasons.push("invalid_url");
  }

  return {
    host,
    suspicious: reasons.length > 0,
    reasons,
  };
}

function toPct(value) {
  return `${(value * 100).toFixed(2)}%`;
}

async function main() {
  const args = parseArgs(process.argv.slice(2));
  const runId = args.runId ?? (await findLatestRunId());
  if (!runId) throw new Error("鏈壘鍒板彲澶嶇洏鐨?run_id銆?);

  const summaryPath = path.join(RAW_ROOT, runId, "run-summary.json");
  if (!(await fileExists(summaryPath))) {
    throw new Error(`鏈壘鍒?run-summary.json: ${summaryPath}`);
  }
  const runSummary = await readJson(summaryPath);
  const summaries = Array.isArray(runSummary.summaries) ? runSummary.summaries : [];
  const expectedSources = args.sources ?? summaries.map((s) => s.source_id);

  const totalCandidate = summaries.reduce((acc, s) => acc + Number(s.candidate_url_count || 0), 0);
  const totalFetched = summaries.reduce((acc, s) => acc + Number(s.fetched_url_count || 0), 0);
  const totalFailed = summaries.reduce((acc, s) => acc + Number(s.failed_url_count || 0), 0);
  const failRate = totalCandidate > 0 ? totalFailed / totalCandidate : 1;

  const sourceChecks = expectedSources.map((sourceId) => {
    const row = summaries.find((s) => s.source_id === sourceId);
    return {
      source_id: sourceId,
      present: Boolean(row),
      fetched_url_count: Number(row?.fetched_url_count || 0),
      failed_url_count: Number(row?.failed_url_count || 0),
      pass: Boolean(row) && Number(row?.fetched_url_count || 0) > 0,
    };
  });
  const passSourceOutput = sourceChecks.every((row) => row.pass);
  const passFailRate = failRate < args.maxFailRate;

  const cleanPath = path.join(CLEAN_ROOT, runId, "tool_entities_preview.jsonl");
  const entities = await readJsonl(cleanPath);
  const sample = sampleRows(entities, Math.max(1, args.sampleSize));
  const sourceHosts = new Set(
    summaries
      .map((s) => parseHost(s.base_url))
      .filter(Boolean)
  );

  const suspiciousRows = sample
    .map((row) => {
      const analyze = analyzeOfficialUrl(String(row.official_url_hint || ""), sourceHosts);
      return {
        source_id: row.source_id,
        page_title: row.page_title,
        official_url_hint: row.official_url_hint,
        host: analyze.host,
        suspicious: analyze.suspicious,
        reasons: analyze.reasons,
      };
    })
    .filter((row) => row.suspicious);

  const sampleSize = sample.length;
  const noiseRate = sampleSize > 0 ? suspiciousRows.length / sampleSize : 1;
  const passNoiseRate = noiseRate < args.maxNoiseRate;
  const filledOfficialCount = entities.filter(
    (row) => String(row.official_url_hint || "").trim().length > 0
  ).length;
  const officialFillRate = entities.length > 0 ? filledOfficialCount / entities.length : 0;
  const passOfficialFillRate = officialFillRate >= args.minOfficialFillRate;

  const report = {
    run_id: runId,
    reviewed_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    thresholds: {
      expected_sources: expectedSources,
      max_fail_rate: args.maxFailRate,
      max_noise_rate: args.maxNoiseRate,
      sample_size: args.sampleSize,
      min_official_fill_rate: args.minOfficialFillRate,
    },
    metrics: {
      total_candidate_url_count: totalCandidate,
      total_fetched_url_count: totalFetched,
      total_failed_url_count: totalFailed,
      fail_rate: failRate,
      fail_rate_text: toPct(failRate),
      clean_entity_count: entities.length,
      sampled_entity_count: sampleSize,
      suspicious_sample_count: suspiciousRows.length,
      suspicious_sample_rate: noiseRate,
      suspicious_sample_rate_text: toPct(noiseRate),
      official_url_filled_count: filledOfficialCount,
      official_url_fill_rate: officialFillRate,
      official_url_fill_rate_text: toPct(officialFillRate),
    },
    gate: {
      source_output_pass: passSourceOutput,
      fail_rate_pass: passFailRate,
      noise_rate_pass: passNoiseRate,
      official_fill_rate_pass: passOfficialFillRate,
      overall_pass: passSourceOutput && passFailRate && passNoiseRate && passOfficialFillRate,
    },
    source_checks: sourceChecks,
    suspicious_samples: suspiciousRows,
  };

  const outDir = path.join(REVIEW_ROOT, runId);
  await ensureDir(outDir);
  const outPath = path.join(outDir, "stage-b-review.json");
  await fs.writeFile(outPath, JSON.stringify(report, null, 2), "utf8");

  console.log(`闃舵B澶嶇洏瀹屾垚: run_id=${runId}`);
  console.log(`source_output_pass=${report.gate.source_output_pass}`);
  console.log(`fail_rate=${report.metrics.fail_rate_text}, pass=${report.gate.fail_rate_pass}`);
  console.log(
    `noise_rate=${report.metrics.suspicious_sample_rate_text} (${report.metrics.suspicious_sample_count}/${report.metrics.sampled_entity_count}), pass=${report.gate.noise_rate_pass}`
  );
  console.log(
    `official_fill_rate=${report.metrics.official_url_fill_rate_text} (${report.metrics.official_url_filled_count}/${report.metrics.clean_entity_count}), pass=${report.gate.official_fill_rate_pass}`
  );
  console.log(`overall_pass=${report.gate.overall_pass}`);
  console.log(`鎶ュ憡杈撳嚭: ${outPath}`);
}

main().catch((err) => {
  console.error(err);
  process.exit(1);
});

function sleep(ms) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

function apiBase(baseUrl) {
  const cleaned = baseUrl.replace(/\/+$/, "");
  return cleaned.endsWith("/api") ? cleaned : `${cleaned}/api`;
}

async function requestJson(url, options = {}) {
  const res = await fetch(url, options);
  const text = await res.text();
  let body = null;
  try {
    body = text ? JSON.parse(text) : null;
  } catch {
    body = null;
  }
  if (!res.ok) {
    const message = body?.message || body?.error || text || `HTTP ${res.status}`;
    throw new Error(`璇锋眰澶辫触 ${url}: ${message}`);
  }
  return body;
}

async function login(args) {
  const base = apiBase(args.baseUrl);
  const body = await requestJson(`${base}/login`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify({ username: args.username, password: args.password }),
  });
  const token = body?.data || "";
  if (!token) throw new Error("Crawlab 鐧诲綍鎴愬姛浣嗘湭杩斿洖 token");
  return { base, token };
}

async function getAll(base, token, path) {
  const data = await requestJson(`${base}${path}${path.includes("?") ? "&" : "?"}all=1`, {
    headers: { Authorization: token },
  });
  return Array.isArray(data?.data) ? data.data : [];
}

async function ensureProject(base, token, projectName) {
  const list = await getAll(base, token, "/projects");
  const existing = list.find((row) => row?.name === projectName);
  if (existing?._id) return existing;
  const created = await requestJson(`${base}/projects`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      Authorization: token,
      "content-type": "application/json",
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      name: projectName,
      description: "Agentree Crawlab integration project",
    }),
  });
  return created?.data;
}

async function ensureCollection(base, token, collectionName) {
  const list = await getAll(base, token, "/data/collections");
  const existing = list.find((row) => row?.name === collectionName);
  if (existing?._id) return existing;
  const created = await requestJson(`${base}/data/collections`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      Authorization: token,
      "content-type": "application/json",
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      name: collectionName,
      description: "Agentree crawler output collection",
    }),
  });
  return created?.data;
}

function spiderPayload(args, projectId, collectionId) {
  return {
    name: args.spiderName,
    type: "",
    col_id: collectionId,
    data_source_id: "000000000000000000000000",
    description: "Run papaweb crawler from Crawlab gateway",
    project_id: projectId ?? "000000000000000000000000",
    mode: args.mode,
    node_ids: null,
    cmd: args.command,
    param: "",
    priority: args.priority,
    incremental_sync: false,
  };
}

async function ensureSpider(base, token, args, projectId, collectionId) {
  const list = await getAll(base, token, "/spiders");
  const existing = list.find((row) => row?.name === args.spiderName);
  const payload = spiderPayload(args, projectId, collectionId);
  if (existing?._id) {
    await requestJson(`${base}/spiders/${existing._id}`, {
      method: "PUT",
      headers: {
        Authorization: token,
        "content-type": "application/json",
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ ...existing, ...payload }),
    });
    return { ...existing, ...payload, _id: existing._id };
  }

  const created = await requestJson(`${base}/spiders`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      Authorization: token,
      "content-type": "application/json",
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(payload),
  });
  return created?.data;
}

async function ensureSpiderWorkspace(base, token, spiderId) {
  if (!spiderId) return;
  try {
    await requestJson(`${base}/spiders/${spiderId}/files/save/dir?path=.`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        Authorization: token,
        "content-type": "application/json",
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ path: "." }),
    });
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn(`[crawlab] workspace init skipped: ${err?.message || err}`);
  }
}

async function runSpider(base, token, spiderId, args) {
  return requestJson(`${base}/spiders/${spiderId}/run`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      Authorization: token,
      "content-type": "application/json",
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      cmd: args.command,
      param: "",
      mode: args.mode,
      priority: args.priority,
    }),
  });
}

async function getLatestSpiderTask(base, token, spiderId) {
  const conditions = encodeURIComponent(
    JSON.stringify([{ key: "spider_id", op: "eq", value: spiderId }])
  );
  const sort = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify([{ key: "create_ts", desc: true }]));
  const url = `${base}/tasks?page=1&size=1&conditions=${conditions}&sort=${sort}`;
  const body = await requestJson(url, {
    headers: { Authorization: token },
  });
  return Array.isArray(body?.data) && body.data.length > 0 ? body.data[0] : null;
}

function isTaskDone(status) {
  return ["finished", "error", "cancelled", "abnormal"].includes(String(status || "").toLowerCase());
}

async function main() {
  const args = parseArgs(process.argv.slice(2));
  const { base, token } = await login(args);
  console.log(`[crawlab] 鐧诲綍鎴愬姛: ${base}`);

  const project = await ensureProject(base, token, args.projectName);
  if (!project?._id) throw new Error("鍒涘缓/鑾峰彇 Crawlab project 澶辫触");
  console.log(`[crawlab] project=${project.name} id=${project._id}`);

  const collection = await ensureCollection(base, token, args.collectionName);
  if (!collection?._id) throw new Error("鍒涘缓/鑾峰彇 Crawlab results collection 澶辫触");
  console.log(`[crawlab] collection=${collection.name} id=${collection._id}`);

  const spider = await ensureSpider(base, token, args, project._id, collection._id);
  if (!spider?._id) throw new Error("鍒涘缓/鏇存柊 Crawlab spider 澶辫触");
  console.log(`[crawlab] spider=${spider.name} id=${spider._id}`);
  console.log(`[crawlab] cmd=${args.command}`);

  await ensureSpiderWorkspace(base, token, spider._id);

  await runSpider(base, token, spider._id, args);
  console.log("[crawlab] 浠诲姟宸茶Е鍙戙€?);
  if (args.noWait || args.waitSeconds <= 0) {
    console.log("[crawlab] no-wait enabled; exit after trigger.");
    return;
  }
  console.log("[crawlab] 寮€濮嬭疆璇㈢姸鎬?..");

  const deadline = Date.now() + args.waitSeconds * 1000;
  let latest = null;
  while (Date.now() < deadline) {
    latest = await getLatestSpiderTask(base, token, spider._id);
    if (latest) {
      const status = String(latest.status || "unknown");
      console.log(`[crawlab] task=${latest._id} status=${status}`);
      if (isTaskDone(status)) break;
    } else {
      console.log("[crawlab] 鏆傛棤浠诲姟璁板綍锛岀户缁瓑寰?..");
    }
    await sleep(Math.max(1, args.pollSeconds) * 1000);
  }

  if (!latest) {
    throw new Error("鏈煡璇㈠埌浠诲姟璁板綍锛岃妫€鏌?Crawlab worker 鏄惁鍦ㄧ嚎銆?);
  }

  const finalStatus = String(latest.status || "unknown").toLowerCase();
  if (!isTaskDone(finalStatus)) {
    throw new Error(`浠诲姟瓒呮椂鏈粨鏉燂紝褰撳墠鐘舵€?${latest.status}`);
  }
  if (finalStatus !== "finished") {
    throw new Error(`浠诲姟鎵ц澶辫触锛岀姸鎬?${latest.status}`);
  }

  console.log("[crawlab] 浠诲姟鎵ц瀹屾垚锛岀姸鎬?finished");
}

main().catch((err) => {
  console.error(err);
  process.exit(1);
});

QUERY_API_BASE_URL = os.environ.get("PAPAWEB_QUERY_API_INTERNAL_URL", "http://query-api:18787").rstrip("/")


def _http_get(path: str) -> dict:
  req = urllib.request.Request(f"{QUERY_API_BASE_URL}{path}", method="GET")
  with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=30) as resp:
    body = resp.read().decode("utf-8")
    if resp.status < 200 or resp.status >= 300:
      raise RuntimeError(f"GET {path} failed status={resp.status} body={body}")
    return json.loads(body) if body else {}


def _http_post(path: str, payload: dict) -> dict:
  data = json.dumps(payload).encode("utf-8")
  req = urllib.request.Request(
    f"{QUERY_API_BASE_URL}{path}",
    data=data,
    method="POST",
    headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
  )

    body = resp.read().decode("utf-8")

    return json.loads(body) if body else {}

# papaweb

面向“工具导航网站”场景的采集/清洗/复盘闭环 Monorepo。当前重点是 `apps/crawler`，调度用 Crawlab，渲染用 Pinchtab。

**核心入口**
- 采集入口：`apps/crawler/src/collect.mjs`
- Crawlab 调度入口：`apps/crawler/src/run-via-crawlab.mjs`
- 站点规则：`apps/crawler/config/source-sites.v1.json`
- 字段 schema：`apps/crawler/config/field-schema.v1.json`
- 源码部署：`infra/docker/`（Crawlab + Pinchtab 源码构建）

**Plan0 平台化最小闭环**
- Worker：`services/worker-seed`、`services/worker-fetch-http`、`services/worker-normalize`、`services/worker-quality`、`services/publish_worker`
- Query API：`services/query-api`
- Airflow DAG：`services/orchestrator-airflow/dags/papaweb_platform_seed_pipeline.py`
- 共享包：`packages/contracts`、`packages/policy-engine`、`packages/shared`
- Docker 分层：`infra/docker/compose.platform.yml`（通过 Stage D 启动）

    src/
    tests/
infra/
  docker/
docs/
  plan/

**Stage D 一键启动（平台闭环）**
```powershell
cd D:\demo1\papaweb\infra\docker
.\start.ps1 -Stage D -WithGrafana $true -Build
.\healthcheck.ps1 -Stage D -WithGrafana $true
.\platform-smoke.ps1 -TimeoutSec 300 -MinPublished 1
```

**方法一：本地 CLI 采集**
1. 安装 Node.js `>=18`。
2. 可选：启动 Crawlab + Pinchtab（需要渲染时再开）。
```powershell
cd D:\demo1\papaweb\infra\docker
.\bootstrap.ps1
```
```bash
docker compose up -d --build
```
3. 运行采集（示例：三站各 1000 条）。
```bash
node apps/crawler/src/collect.mjs --once --source futurepedia,toolify,ainav_cn --max-urls-per-source 1000 --revisit-hours 0 --pinchtab-url http://127.0.0.1:19867
```
4. 查看输出。
```text
apps/crawler/data/raw/<run_id>/
```

**方法二：Crawlab 调度采集**
1. 启动 Crawlab + Pinchtab（同上）。
2. 打开 Crawlab UI：`http://127.0.0.1:18080`（默认 `admin/admin`）。
3. 通过脚本自动创建项目/爬虫并触发任务。
```bash
node apps/crawler/src/run-via-crawlab.mjs
```
4. 覆盖采集参数（示例：三站各 1000 条，容器内 Pinchtab 地址为 `http://pinchtab:9867`）。
```bash
node apps/crawler/src/run-via-crawlab.mjs --command "node /workspace/apps/crawler/src/collect.mjs --once --source futurepedia,toolify,ainav_cn --max-urls-per-source 1000 --revisit-hours 0 --pinchtab-url http://pinchtab:9867 --pinchtab-token papaweb-local-token"
```
5. 如需自定义 token：修改 `infra/docker/docker-compose.yml` 的 `PINCHTAB_TOKEN`，并在命令里同步更新 `--pinchtab-token`。

**常用参数**
- `--pinchtab-url http://127.0.0.1:19867`
- `--pinchtab-mode always|fallback|disable`
- `--pinchtab-token <token>`（若 Pinchtab 开启了 auth）
- `--delay-min-ms 1200 --delay-max-ms 1800`
- `--max-failures 200 --max-consecutive-failures 20`
- `--source-concurrency 3`

**输出目录**
- 原始下载：`apps/crawler/data/raw/<run_id>/`
- 清洗结果：`apps/crawler/data/clean/<run_id>/`
- 复盘报告：`apps/crawler/data/review/<run_id>/`

**采集边界**
- 仅抓取公开页面与 robots 允许路径。
- 不登录、不绕过付费墙、不模拟注册。
- 对 `Disallow: /` 的源自动跳过。

**文档**
- `apps/crawler/README.md`
- `infra/docker/README.md`
- `docs/plan/工具导航网站整体架构蓝图.md`
- `docs/plan/工具导航网站采集流程复盘与注意事项.md`

Output:
# Docker Deployment (Layered Compose)

This directory now supports a layered deployment model for Plan0.
The rule is: one service, one container. Do not put all services in one container.

This is the common pattern used by large open-source products (including workflow/AI platforms): split web, worker, db, queue, and observability into separate containers and compose them by environment.

## Compose files

- `compose.base.yml`: PostgreSQL + Valkey + SeaweedFS
- `compose.collect.yml`: Crawlab + Pinchtab (+ Mongo for Crawlab)
- `compose.orchestrator.yml`: Airflow (init + webserver + scheduler)
- `compose.observability.yml`: Prometheus + Alertmanager (+ optional Grafana)
- `compose.platform.yml`: platform workers (`seed/fetch/normalize/quality/publish`) + query API
- `docker-compose.yml`: legacy single-file source-build entry kept for compatibility

## 1) Prepare

```powershell
cd D:\demo1\papaweb\infra\docker
Copy-Item .env.example .env -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
.\bootstrap.ps1
```

## 2) Validate compose merge

```bash
docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.collect.yml config -q
```

## 3) Start by stage

### Stage A: collection stack (recommended first step)

```bash
docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.collect.yml up -d --build
```

### Stage B: add orchestrator (Airflow)

```bash
docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.collect.yml -f compose.orchestrator.yml up -d --build
```

### Stage C: add observability

```bash
docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.collect.yml -f compose.orchestrator.yml -f compose.observability.yml up -d --build
```

### Stage D: add platform workers + query API

```bash
docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.collect.yml -f compose.orchestrator.yml -f compose.observability.yml -f compose.platform.yml up -d --build
```

### Optional: enable Grafana profile

```bash
docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.collect.yml -f compose.orchestrator.yml -f compose.observability.yml --profile grafana up -d --build
```

## One-Click Scripts (PowerShell)

```powershell
# start full stack (Stage C + Grafana)
.\start.ps1 -Stage C -WithGrafana $true -Build

# start full stack + platform workers (Stage D + Grafana)
.\start.ps1 -Stage D -WithGrafana $true -Build

# health check
.\healthcheck.ps1 -Stage D -WithGrafana $true

# smoke check (will trigger one seed run via query-api)
.\platform-smoke.ps1 -TimeoutSec 300 -MinPublished 1

# stop stack
.\stop.ps1 -Stage D -WithGrafana $true
```

Optional examples:

```powershell
# Stage A only
.\start.ps1 -Stage A -WithGrafana $false -Build
.\healthcheck.ps1 -Stage A -WithGrafana $false

# stop and remove volumes
.\stop.ps1 -Stage C -WithGrafana $true -RemoveVolumes
```

## 4) Stop

```bash
docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.collect.yml -f compose.orchestrator.yml -f compose.observability.yml --profile grafana down
```

## Service endpoints (default)

- Crawlab UI: `http://127.0.0.1:18080`
- Pinchtab: `http://127.0.0.1:19867`
- Airflow UI: `http://127.0.0.1:18081`
- Prometheus: `http://127.0.0.1:19090`
- Alertmanager: `http://127.0.0.1:19093`
- Grafana (optional profile): `http://127.0.0.1:13000`
- SeaweedFS filer: `http://127.0.0.1:18888`
- Query API: `http://127.0.0.1:18787`

## Airflow DAG (Stage D)

- DAG file: `services/orchestrator-airflow/dags/papaweb_platform_seed_pipeline.py`
- Runtime behavior: Airflow triggers `POST /api/v1/pipeline/seed-run` on `query-api`, then snapshots `GET /api/v1/metrics`.
- Manual trigger:
```bash
docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.collect.yml -f compose.orchestrator.yml -f compose.observability.yml -f compose.platform.yml --profile grafana exec -T airflow-webserver airflow dags trigger papaweb_platform_seed_pipeline
```

## Notes

- Runtime data is stored in `infra/docker/data/`.
- Keep `docker-compose.yml` only for legacy compatibility; use layered files for all new deployments.
- `Kafka`, `OpenSearch`, `ClickHouse`, `Superset` are intentionally not in the default boot path and should be enabled by workload/RFC gates.
- Stage D validates the Plan0 minimal closed loop: `fetch -> normalize -> quality -> publish`.

param(
  [int]$TimeoutSec = 240,
  [int]$MinPublished = 1,
  [switch]$SkipTriggerSeed
)

$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"

$root = Split-Path -Parent $MyInvocation.MyCommand.Path
Set-Location $root

. "$root/_compose-common.ps1"

$envMap = Get-EnvMap -Path ".env"
$portQueryApi = Get-EnvOrDefault -EnvMap $envMap -Key "PAPAWEB_QUERY_API_PORT" -DefaultValue "18787"
$metricsUrl = "http://127.0.0.1:$portQueryApi/api/v1/metrics"
$toolsUrl = "http://127.0.0.1:$portQueryApi/api/v1/tools?limit=5"
$triggerUrl = "http://127.0.0.1:$portQueryApi/api/v1/pipeline/seed-run"

$deadline = (Get-Date).AddSeconds($TimeoutSec)
$success = $false

Write-Host "Platform smoke check started (timeout=${TimeoutSec}s, minPublished=${MinPublished})"

if (-not $SkipTriggerSeed) {
  try {
    $payload = @{
      requestedBy = "platform-smoke"
      reason = "smoke_check"
    } | ConvertTo-Json -Compress
    $triggerResult = Invoke-RestMethod -Uri $triggerUrl -Method Post -ContentType "application/json" -Body $payload -TimeoutSec 10
    Write-Host "seed trigger accepted: jobId=$($triggerResult.jobId) seedCount=$($triggerResult.seedCount)"
  } catch {
    Write-Host "seed trigger failed: $($_.Exception.Message)"
    exit 1
  }
}

while ((Get-Date) -lt $deadline) {
  try {
    $metrics = Invoke-RestMethod -Uri $metricsUrl -Method Get -TimeoutSec 8
    $published = [int]$metrics.publishedTasks
    $total = [int]$metrics.totalTasks
    Write-Host "metrics: total=$total published=$published"
    if ($published -ge $MinPublished) {
      $success = $true
      break
    }
  } catch {
    Write-Host "waiting query-api: $($_.Exception.Message)"
  }
  Start-Sleep -Seconds 5
}

if (-not $success) {
  Write-Host "Platform smoke check FAILED: publishedTasks < $MinPublished within ${TimeoutSec}s"
  exit 1
}

if ($tools.items) {
  foreach ($item in $tools.items) {
    Write-Host "- [$($item.id)] $($item.title) -> $($item.canonical_url)"
  }
}

exit 0

function Test-HttpEndpoint {
  param(
    [string]$Name,
    [string]$Url,
    [int]$Retries = 3,
    [int]$DelaySec = 2
  )

  for ($attempt = 1; $attempt -le $Retries; $attempt++) {
    try {
      $res = Invoke-WebRequest -Uri $Url -Method Get -TimeoutSec 8
      if ($res.StatusCode -ge 200 -and $res.StatusCode -lt 400) {
        Write-Host "[OK] HTTP $Name -> $Url ($($res.StatusCode))"
        return $true
      }
      Write-Host "[WARN] HTTP $Name attempt=$attempt/$Retries -> status=$($res.StatusCode)"
    } catch {
      Write-Host "[WARN] HTTP $Name attempt=$attempt/$Retries -> $($_.Exception.Message)"
    }

    if ($attempt -lt $Retries) {
      Start-Sleep -Seconds $DelaySec
    }
  }

  Write-Host "[FAIL] HTTP $Name -> $Url"
  return $false
}

function Test-ServiceState {
  param(
    [string]$Service,
    [bool]$RequireHealthy = $false
  )
  $id = (docker compose @composeArgs ps -q $Service).Trim()
  if ([string]::IsNullOrWhiteSpace($id)) {
    Write-Host "[FAIL] Service $Service not found"
    return $false
  }

  $state = (docker inspect --format '{{.State.Status}}' $id).Trim()
  if ($state -ne "running") {
    Write-Host "[FAIL] Service $Service state=$state"
    return $false
  }

  if ($RequireHealthy) {
    $health = (docker inspect --format '{{if .State.Health}}{{.State.Health.Status}}{{else}}none{{end}}' $id).Trim()
    if ($health -ne "healthy") {
      Write-Host "[FAIL] Service $Service health=$health"
      return $false
    }
  }

  Write-Host "[OK] Service $Service running"
  return $true
}

 158: function normalizeLimit(value, defaultValue, max) {
 159:   const n = Number(value);
 160:   if (!Number.isFinite(n) || n <= 0) return defaultValue;
 161:   return Math.min(Math.floor(n), max);
 162: }
 163: 
 164: function normalizeArray(value) {
 165:   if (Array.isArray(value)) {
 166:     return value.map((item) => String(item).trim()).filter(Boolean);
 167:   }
 168:   if (typeof value === "string") {
 169:     return value
 170:       .split(",")
 171:       .map((item) => item.trim())
 172:       .filter(Boolean);
 173:   }
 174:   return [];
 175: }
 176: 
 177: function normalizeString(value) {
 178:   if (typeof value !== "string") return "";
 179:   return value.trim();
 180: }

  26: async function fetchHtml(url) {
  27:   const ctrl = new AbortController();
  28:   const timer = setTimeout(() => ctrl.abort(), config.fetchTimeoutMs);
  29:   try {
  30:     const res = await fetch(url, {
  31:       method: "GET",
  32:       redirect: "follow",
  33:       signal: ctrl.signal,

  35:         "user-agent": "papaweb-platform/0.1",
  36:       },
  37:     });
  38:     const text = await res.text();
  39:     return {
  40:       ok: res.ok,
  41:       status: res.status,
  42:       html: text.slice(0, 250000),
  43:       error: null,
  44:     };
  45:   } catch (error) {
  46:     return {
  47:       ok: false,
  48:       status: 0,
  49:       html: "",
  50:       error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
  51:     };

  26: function pickTitle(html, url) {
  27:   const titleMatch = html.match(/<title[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/title>/i);
  28:   const title = (titleMatch?.[1] ?? "").replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim();
  29:   if (title.length > 0) return title.slice(0, 200);
  30:   return url;
  31: }
  32: 
  33: function pickSummary(html) {
  34:   const metaMatch =
  35:     html.match(/<meta[^>]*name=["']description["'][^>]*content=["']([\s\S]*?)["'][^>]*>/i) ||
  36:     html.match(/<meta[^>]*content=["']([\s\S]*?)["'][^>]*name=["']description["'][^>]*>/i);
  37:   if (metaMatch?.[1]) {
  38:     return metaMatch[1].replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim().slice(0, 300);
  39:   }
  40:   const bodyText = html
  41:     .replace(/<script[\s\S]*?<\/script>/gi, " ")
  42:     .replace(/<style[\s\S]*?<\/style>/gi, " ")
  43:     .replace(/<[^>]+>/g, " ")
  44:     .replace(/\s+/g, " ")
  45:     .trim();
  46:   return bodyText.slice(0, 300);
  47: }
  48: 
  49: async function processMessage(pg, redis, message) {
  50:   const traceId = requireString(message.traceId, "traceId");
  51:   const jobId = requireString(message.jobId, "jobId");
  52:   const taskId = requireString(message.taskId, "taskId");

  56: 
  57:   const taskRes = await pg.query("SELECT raw_html FROM crawl_tasks WHERE id = $1 LIMIT 1", [taskId]);
  58:   if (taskRes.rowCount === 0) {
  59:     throw new Error(`task not found: ${taskId}`);
  60:   }
  61:   const html = String(taskRes.rows[0].raw_html ?? "");

  63:     canonicalUrl: url,
  64:     title: pickTitle(html, url),
  65:     summary: pickSummary(html),
  66:     sourceId,
  67:     normalizedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  68:   };
  69: 
  70:   await pg.query(
  71:     `UPDATE crawl_tasks
  72:      SET stage = $2, status = $3, normalized = $4::jsonb, updated_at = NOW()
  73:      WHERE id = $1`,

  78: export async function ensurePlatformSchema(pg) {
  79:   const lockKey = 20260313;
  80:   const sql = `
  81:     CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS crawl_jobs (
  82:       id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  83:       source_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  84:       status TEXT NOT NULL,
  85:       created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  86:       updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
  87:     );
  88: 
  89:     CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS crawl_tasks (
  90:       id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  91:       job_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES crawl_jobs(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  92:       trace_id TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  93:       source_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  94:       url TEXT NOT NULL,
  95:       stage TEXT NOT NULL,
  96:       status TEXT NOT NULL,
  97:       error TEXT,
  98:       http_status INT,
  99:       raw_html TEXT,
 100:       normalized JSONB,
 101:       quality JSONB,
 102:       published BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
 103:       created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
 104:       updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
 105:     );

 180:   `;

 184:   } finally {
 185:     await pg.query("SELECT pg_advisory_unlock($1)", [lockKey]);
 186:   }
